######SETUP EVENTS######

#Lepsius 2: Lepsius' letter to Rosellini: Adds state modifiers to Upper and Lower Egypt and thus makes excavations possible

lepsius.2 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.2.t
	desc = lepsius.2.d
	flavor = lepsius.2.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/egypt/lepsius_egypt_giza.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		create_lepsius_karl_richard_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.2.a #We will explore the wonders of Egypt!
		custom_tooltip = lepsius.2.tt
		s:STATE_LOWER_EGYPT = {
			add_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_lower_egypt
		}
		s:STATE_UPPER_EGYPT = {
			add_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_upper_egypt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_player = no
			}
			c:EGY = {
				change_relations = {
					country = ROOT 
					value = 15
				}
			}
			create_diplomatic_pact = {
				country = c:EGY
				type = excavation_license
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			post_notification = lepsius_rosellini_notification
		}
		set_global_variable = lepsius_archaeology_possible_global_var
	}
}

#Lepsius 3: Stephens & Catherwood Expedition, access to Guatemala (you need something against malaria, however)

lepsius.3 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.3.t
	desc = lepsius.3.d
	flavor = lepsius.3.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/yucatan/lepsius_yucatan_plate4_copan.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.3.a #We should stock up on fine leather jackets.
		custom_tooltip = lepsius.3.tt
		s:STATE_YUCATAN = {
			add_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_yucatan
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			post_notification = lepsius_stephens_catherwood_expedition_notification
		}
		set_global_variable = lepsius_archaeology_possible_global_var
	}
}

#Lepsius 4: Decipherment of the Akkadian language, access to Babylonia and Assyria (early archaeology is needed)

lepsius.4 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.4.t
	desc = lepsius.4.d
	flavor = lepsius.4.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/mesopotamia/lepsius_mesopotamia_nimrud.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = lepsius_decipherment_akkadian_var
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.4.a #We should stock up on fine leather jackets.
		custom_tooltip = lepsius.4.tt
		s:STATE_BAGHDAD = {
			add_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_babylonia
		}
		s:STATE_MOSUL = {
			add_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_assyria
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			post_notification = lepsius_decipherment_akkadian_notification
		}
		set_global_variable = lepsius_archaeology_possible_global_var
	}
}

#Lepsius 5: Schliemann discovers Troy, access to Argolis and Crete (early archaeology for Argolis and modern archaeology for Crete is needed)

lepsius.5 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.5.t
	desc = lepsius.5.d
	flavor = lepsius.5.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/greece/lepsius_greece_schliemann.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = lepsius_support_schliemann_var
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.5.a #Menin aeide, thea, Peleiadeo Achileos ...
		custom_tooltip = lepsius.5.tt
		s:STATE_PELOPONNESE = {
			add_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_argolis
		}
		s:STATE_CRETE = {
			add_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_crete
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			post_notification = lepsius_support_schliemann_notification
		}
		set_global_variable = lepsius_archaeology_possible_global_var
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.741
				years = 10
			}
		}
	}
}

			post_notification = lepsius_machu_picchu_notification
		}
		set_global_variable = lepsius_archaeology_possible_global_var
	}
}

#Lepsius 7: Fiorelli's Excavation of Pompeii

lepsius.7 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.7.t
	desc = lepsius.7.d
	flavor = lepsius.7.f

	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:lepsius_archaeologist_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = lepsius_pompeii_var
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.7.g #We are primarily interested in artifacts.
		lepsius_add_x_local_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 10 }
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.7.h #We want to know more about the past.
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_medium_add_technology = yes
	}

	option = {

		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = {
			AMOUNT = 60
		}

	}
}

#Lepsius 10: Museum Inauguration

lepsius.10 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.10.t

	desc = lepsius.10.d

	flavor = lepsius.10.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/museum/lepsius_museum_interior.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = {
			set_variable = lepsius_museum_inauguration_happened
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var }
			var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
				set_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_inaugurated_museum_var
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.10.g #Visit the new museum
		default_option = yes
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = {
			AMOUNT = "5"
		}
		set_variable = lepsius_visiting_museum_var
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = { 
				id = lepsius.11
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.10.h #Have a nice day
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = {
			AMOUNT = "5"
		}
	}

	after = {
		lepsius_update_exhibition_effect = yes
	}
}

#Lepsius 18: World Cultures Collection

lepsius.18 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.18.t
	desc = lepsius.18.d
	flavor = lepsius.18.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/museum/lepsius_museum_world_cultures_collection.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
		#lepsius_museum_decision
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	#Arrange Far Eastern Exhibition
	option = {
		name = lepsius.18.g
		remove_variable = lepsius_visiting_museum_var
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = lepsius_fareastern_exhibition_var
			}
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_prepare_new_exhibition_modifier
			}
			var:lepsius_fareastern_artifact_minor >= 10
		}
		set_variable = lepsius_fareastern_exhibition_var
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_prepare_new_exhibition_modifier
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
			months = 12
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = { 
				id = lepsius.27
				days = { 160 200 }
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#Arrange Oceanic Exhibition
	option = {
		name = lepsius.18.h
		remove_variable = lepsius_visiting_museum_var
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = lepsius_oceanic_exhibition_var
			}
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_prepare_new_exhibition_modifier
			}
			var:lepsius_oceanic_artifact_minor >= 10
		}
		set_variable = lepsius_oceanic_exhibition_var
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_prepare_new_exhibition_modifier
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
			months = 12
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = { 
				id = lepsius.27
				days = { 160 200 }
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#Back to the Main Hall
	option = {
		name = lepsius.12.k
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = { 
				id = lepsius.11
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#Bye
	option = {
		name = lepsius.12.l
		remove_variable = lepsius_visiting_museum_var
	}
}

#Lepsius 23: Mesopotamian Exhibition #REMOVED

#Lepsius 27: World Cultures Exhibition

lepsius.27 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.27.t
	desc = lepsius.22.d
	flavor = lepsius.22.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/museum/lepsius_museum_world_cultures_collection.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
		#lepsius_museum_decision
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	#New Exhibition
	option = {
		name = lepsius.22.g
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_fareastern_exhibition_var
				has_modifier = lepsius_prepare_new_exhibition_modifier
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_fareastern_exhibition_modifier
				}
			}
			remove_modifier = lepsius_prepare_new_exhibition_modifier
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_fareastern_exhibition_modifier
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_new_exhibition_modifier
				days = 120
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_oceanic_exhibition_var
				has_modifier = lepsius_prepare_new_exhibition_modifier
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_oceanic_exhibition_modifier
				}
			}
			remove_modifier = lepsius_prepare_new_exhibition_modifier
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_oceanic_exhibition_modifier
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_new_exhibition_modifier
				days = 120
			}
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 50: Yearly excavation report

lepsius.50 = {
	type = country_event
		
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = lepsius_excavation_artifacts_cooldown_var
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = lepsius_excavation_artifacts_cooldown_var
			days = 365
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_upper_egypt_excavation_modifier #Valley of the Kings
				NOT = {
					any_state = {
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_upper_egypt
						has_modifier = lepsius_excavation_sacked_state_modifier
					}
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_egyptian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_lower_egypt_excavation_modifier #The Pyramids
				NOT = {
					any_state = {
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_lower_egypt
						has_modifier = lepsius_excavation_sacked_state_modifier
					}
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_egyptian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_babylonia_excavation_modifier #Babylon
				NOT = {
					any_state = {
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_babylonia
						has_modifier = lepsius_excavation_sacked_state_modifier
					}
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_mesopotamian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 1}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_assyria_excavation_modifier #Assyria
				NOT = {
					any_state = {
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_assyria
						has_modifier = lepsius_excavation_sacked_state_modifier
					}
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_mesopotamian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 1}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_babylonia_excavation_modifier #Babylon
				has_modifier = lepsius_panbabylonism_modifier  ##Gives +2 excavation artifacts each year
				NOT = {
					any_state = {
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_babylonia
						has_modifier = lepsius_excavation_sacked_state_modifier
					}
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_mesopotamian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 1}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_assyria_excavation_modifier #Assyria
				has_modifier = lepsius_panbabylonism_modifier  ##Gives +2 excavation artifacts each year
				NOT = {
					any_state = {
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_assyria
						has_modifier = lepsius_excavation_sacked_state_modifier
					}
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_mesopotamian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 1}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_argolis_excavation_modifier #Argolis
				NOT = {
					any_state = {
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_argolis
						has_modifier = lepsius_excavation_sacked_state_modifier
					}
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_aegean_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_crete_excavation_modifier #Crete
				NOT = {
					any_state = {
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_crete
						has_modifier = lepsius_excavation_sacked_state_modifier
					}
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_aegean_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_argolis_excavation_modifier #Argolis
				has_modifier = lepsius_troy_homeric_modifier ##Gives +2 excavation artifacts each year
				NOT = {
					any_state = {
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_argolis
						has_modifier = lepsius_excavation_sacked_state_modifier
					}
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_aegean_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_crete_excavation_modifier #Crete
				has_modifier = lepsius_troy_homeric_modifier ##Gives +2 excavation artifacts each year
				NOT = {
					any_state = {
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_crete
						has_modifier = lepsius_excavation_sacked_state_modifier
					}
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_aegean_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_yucatan_excavation_modifier #Yucatán
				NOT = {
					any_state = {
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_yucatan
						has_modifier = lepsius_excavation_sacked_state_modifier
					}
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_precolumbian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 1}
		}
		if = {

				NOT = {
					any_state = {

					}
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_precolumbian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 1}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_local_excavation_modifier #Local Excavation
			}
			lepsius_add_x_local_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 1}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_on_archaeological_excavation = yes #Notification
			}
			post_notification = lepsius_excavation_artifacts_notification
		}
	}

	after = {
		lepsius_update_exhibition_effect = yes
	}
}

#Lepsius 61: Sack an archaeological excavation

lepsius.61 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.61.t

	desc = lepsius.61.d

	flavor = lepsius.61.f

	placement = ROOT

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/egypt/lepsius_egypt_franco_tuscan_expedition.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
		any_state = {
			controller = ROOT
			NOT = {
				owner = ROOT
			}
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_excavation_sacked_state_modifier
			}
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_excavation_protected_state_modifier
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_upper_egypt
					any_country = {
						has_modifier = lepsius_upper_egypt_excavation_modifier
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_lower_egypt
					any_country = {
						has_modifier = lepsius_lower_egypt_excavation_modifier
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_babylonia
					any_country = {
						has_modifier = lepsius_babylonia_excavation_modifier
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_assyria
					any_country = {
						has_modifier = lepsius_assyria_excavation_modifier
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_argolis
					any_country = {
						has_modifier = lepsius_argolis_excavation_modifier
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_crete
					any_country = {
						has_modifier = lepsius_crete_excavation_modifier
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_yucatan
					any_country = {
						has_modifier = lepsius_yucatan_excavation_modifier
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_peru
					any_country = {
						has_modifier = lepsius_peru_excavation_modifier
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_state = {
			limit = {
				controller = ROOT
				NOT = {
					owner = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_excavation_sacked_state_modifier
				}
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_excavation_protected_state_modifier
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_upper_egypt
						any_country = {
							has_modifier = lepsius_upper_egypt_excavation_modifier
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_lower_egypt
						any_country = {
							has_modifier = lepsius_lower_egypt_excavation_modifier
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_babylonia
						any_country = {
							has_modifier = lepsius_babylonia_excavation_modifier
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_assyria
						any_country = {
							has_modifier = lepsius_assyria_excavation_modifier
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_argolis
						any_country = {
							has_modifier = lepsius_argolis_excavation_modifier
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_crete
						any_country = {
							has_modifier = lepsius_crete_excavation_modifier
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_yucatan
						any_country = {
							has_modifier = lepsius_yucatan_excavation_modifier
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_peru
						any_country = {
							has_modifier = lepsius_peru_excavation_modifier
						}
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_excavation_state
		}
	}

	option = { #Plunder the site!
		name = lepsius.61.g
		default_option = yes
		change_infamy = 3
		scope:lepsius_excavation_state = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_excavation_sacked_state_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:lepsius_excavation_state = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_upper_egypt
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_egyptian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 5 }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_upper_egypt_excavation_modifier
					NOT = {
						this = ROOT
					}
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = lepsius.62
				}
				change_relations = {
					country = ROOT 
					value = -10
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:lepsius_excavation_state = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_lower_egypt
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_egyptian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 5 }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_lower_egypt_excavation_modifier
					NOT = {
						this = ROOT
					}
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = lepsius.62
				}
				change_relations = {
					country = ROOT 
					value = -10
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:lepsius_excavation_state = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_babylonia
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_mesopotamian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 5 }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_babylonia_excavation_modifier
					NOT = {
						this = ROOT
					}
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = lepsius.62
				}
				change_relations = {
					country = ROOT 
					value = -10
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:lepsius_excavation_state = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_assyria
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_mesopotamian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 5 }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_assyria_excavation_modifier
					NOT = {
						this = ROOT
					}
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = lepsius.62
				}
				change_relations = {
					country = ROOT 
					value = -10
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:lepsius_excavation_state = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_argolis
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_aegean_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 5 }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_argolis_excavation_modifier
					NOT = {
						this = ROOT
					}
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = lepsius.62
				}
				change_relations = {
					country = ROOT 
					value = -10
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:lepsius_excavation_state = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_crete
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_aegean_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 5 }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_crete_excavation_modifier
					NOT = {
						this = ROOT
					}
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = lepsius.62
				}
				change_relations = {
					country = ROOT 
					value = -10
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:lepsius_excavation_state = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_yucatan
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_precolumbian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 5 }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_yucatan_excavation_modifier
					NOT = {
						this = ROOT
					}
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = lepsius.62
				}
				change_relations = {
					country = ROOT 
					value = -10
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:lepsius_excavation_state = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_peru
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_precolumbian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 5 }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_peru_excavation_modifier
					NOT = {
						this = ROOT
					}
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = lepsius.62
				}
				change_relations = {
					country = ROOT 
					value = -10
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Remain civilized
		name = lepsius.61.h
		change_infamy = -3
		scope:lepsius_excavation_state = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_excavation_protected_state_modifier 
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Lepsius 70: The Tomb of the First Emperor

lepsius.70 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.70.t
	desc = lepsius.70.d
	flavor = lepsius.70.f

	placement = scope:lepsius_xian_state

	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:lepsius_archaeologist_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_XIAN
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_xian_state
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.70.g #We are primarily interested in artifacts.
		lepsius_add_x_fareastern_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 15 }
		lepsius_add_x_local_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 25 }
		lepsius_large_add_technology = yes
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 30 }
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = {
			AMOUNT = 60
		}
	}

	after = {
		lepsius_update_exhibition_effect = yes
	}
}

			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_GUATEMALA

#Lepsius 80: A new Age of Archaeology! (if Early Archaeology is discovered)
lepsius.80 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.80.t

	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_early_archaeology_focus_egypt
			}
			desc = lepsius.80.d_egypt
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_early_archaeology_focus_mesopotamia
			}
			desc = lepsius.80.d_mesopotamia
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_early_archaeology_focus_aegean
			}
			desc = lepsius.80.d_aegean
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_early_archaeology_focus_precolumbian
			}
			desc = lepsius.80.d_precolumbian
		}
	}

	flavor = lepsius.80.f

	placement = ROOT

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:lepsius_archaeologist_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
		has_technology_researched = lepsius_early_archaeology_tech
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = lepsius_early_archaeology_global_var
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = lepsius_early_archaeology_global_var
		if = {
			limit ={
				NOT = {
					has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
				}
			}
			create_new_archaeologist_effect = yes
			lepsius_set_new_archaeologist_as_archaeologist_effect = yes
		}
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			set_variable = lepsius_invented_early_archaeology_var
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
		set_variable = lepsius_first_invented_early_archaeology_var

		random_list = {
			1 = {
				set_variable = lepsius_early_archaeology_focus_egypt
			}
			1 = {
				set_variable = lepsius_early_archaeology_focus_mesopotamia
			}
			1 = {
				set_variable = lepsius_early_archaeology_focus_aegean
			}
			1 = {
				set_variable = lepsius_early_archaeology_focus_precolumbian
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #So civilized!
		name = lepsius.80.g
		default_option = yes

		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 30 }

		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = lepsius_early_archaeology_focus_egypt }
			lepsius_add_x_egyptian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 5 }
			remove_variable = lepsius_early_archaeology_focus_egypt
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = lepsius_early_archaeology_focus_mesopotamia }
			lepsius_add_x_mesopotamian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 5 }
			remove_variable = lepsius_early_archaeology_focus_mesopotamia
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = lepsius_early_archaeology_focus_aegean }
			lepsius_add_x_aegean_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 5 }
			remove_variable = lepsius_early_archaeology_focus_aegean
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = lepsius_early_archaeology_focus_precolumbian }
			lepsius_add_x_precolumbian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 5 }
			remove_variable = lepsius_early_archaeology_focus_precolumbian
		}
	}

	after = {
		lepsius_update_exhibition_effect = yes
	}
}

#Lepsius 81: Modern Excavation Methods (if Modern Archaeology is discovered)
lepsius.81 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.81.t

	desc = lepsius.81.d

	flavor = lepsius.81.f

	placement = ROOT

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:lepsius_archaeologist_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_anthropology.dds"

	trigger = {
		has_technology_researched = lepsius_modern_archaeology_tech
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = lepsius_modern_archaeology_global_var
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = lepsius_modern_archaeology_global_var
		if = {
			limit ={
				NOT = {
					has_variable = lepsius_anthropologist_var
				}
			}
			create_new_anthropologist_effect = yes
			lepsius_set_new_anthropologist_as_anthropologist_effect = yes
		}
		var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
			set_variable = lepsius_invented_modern_archaeology_var
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = { #We are no longer tomb raiders!
		name = lepsius.81.g
		default_option = yes

		anthropologist_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 30 }

		lepsius_add_x_human_fossils_effect = { AMOUNT = 5 }
		lepsius_change_anthropological_rating = { AMOUNT = 5 }
	}

	after = {
	}
}

		video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_london_center.bk2"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	#3 year Expedition
	option = {
		name = lepsius.100.g
		set_variable = lepsius_long_expedition_var
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_large_expedition_cost
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_medium
		}
		custom_tooltip = lepsius_long_expedition_tt
	}

	#2 year Expedition
	option = {
		name = lepsius.100.h
		default_option = yes
		set_variable = lepsius_medium_expedition_var
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_medium_expedition_cost
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_small
		}
		custom_tooltip = lepsius_medium_expedition_tt
	}

	#1 year Expedition
	option = {
		name = lepsius.100.i
		set_variable = lepsius_short_expedition_var
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_small_expedition_cost
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
		}
		custom_tooltip = lepsius_short_expedition_tt
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = { 
				id = lepsius.120
				days = { 7 14 }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 110: Choose a leader #REMOVED

#Lepsius 120: Military Attaché

lepsius.120 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = ROOT

    title = lepsius.120.t
    desc = lepsius.120.d
    flavor = lepsius.120.f

    event_image = {
		video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_before_the_battle.bk2"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/middleeast/jungle_expedition"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

    duration = 3

	trigger = {
		any_scope_character = {
			OR = {
				has_role = general
				has_role = admiral
			}
			is_busy = no
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_role = general
					has_role = admiral
				}
				is_busy = no
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_military_attache_1
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_role = general
					has_role = admiral
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_military_attache_1
				}
				is_busy = no
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_military_attache_2
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_role = general
					has_role = admiral
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_military_attache_1
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_military_attache_2
				}
				is_busy = no
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_military_attache_3
		}
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.120.g
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:lepsius_military_attache_1
		}
		scope:lepsius_military_attache_1 = {
			set_variable = lepsius_military_attache_var
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.120.h
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:lepsius_military_attache_2
		}
		scope:lepsius_military_attache_2 = {
			set_variable = lepsius_military_attache_var
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.120.i
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:lepsius_military_attache_3
		}
		scope:lepsius_military_attache_3 = {
			set_variable = lepsius_military_attache_var
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_arts_academy
						level >= 3
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { 
					id = lepsius.130
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
							has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_experienced
						}
						scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
							has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_famous
						}
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { 
					id = lepsius.140
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					any_scope_state = {
						is_production_method_active = {
							building_type = building_university
							production_method = pm_dubois_university_mathematics
						}
					}
					literacy_rate >= 0.75
					has_technology_researched = lepsius_modern_archaeology_tech
				}
				trigger_event = { 
					id = lepsius.150
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				trigger_event = { 
					id = lepsius.200
					days = { 50 60 }
					popup = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	event_image = { #Greece
		trigger = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_greece = yes
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/greece/lepsius_greece_beast_burden.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #South America
		trigger = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_south_america = yes
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/south_america/lepsius_south_america_beast_burden.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/middleeast/jungle_expedition"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_military_attache_effect = yes
	}
		
	option = { #We could use some interpreters (more artifacts in the end)
		name = lepsius.210.a
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_expedition_success_large_add = yes	
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
	}
	option = { #We need a guide who knows the secrets of the area (more special events)
		name = lepsius.210.b
		custom_tooltip = lepsius_expedition_mysterious_guide_tt
		set_variable = lepsius_mysterious_guide_var
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						lepsius_has_experienced_archaeologist = yes
						lepsius_has_famous_archaeologist = yes
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { #Archaeologist buys artifacts
					id = lepsius.220
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = cautious
							has_trait = romantic
						}
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { #Romantic writes diary
					id = lepsius.230
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = innovative
							has_trait = meticulous
						}
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { #Innovative writes scientific paper
					id = lepsius.240
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = reckless
							has_trait = wrathful
							has_trait = cruel
						}
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { #Tavern fight
					id = lepsius.250
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = charismatic
							has_trait = tactful
							has_trait = brave
						}
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { #Appreciation
					id = lepsius.260
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
						has_trait = hedonist
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { #Ice cream and Lemonade
					id = lepsius.270
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = basic_diplomat
							has_trait = experienced_diplomat
							has_trait = masterful_diplomat
						}
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { #An audience
					id = lepsius.280
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = resupply_commander
							has_trait = expert_artillery_commander
							has_trait = expert_offensive_planner
							has_trait = expert_defensive_strategist
						}
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { #Attaché 
					id = lepsius.290
					days = { 10 20 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				trigger_event = { #Expedition starts
					id = lepsius.300
					days = { 30 40 }
					popup = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 220: Archaeologist buys artifacts

lepsius.220 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.220.t
	desc = lepsius.220.d

	flavor = lepsius.220.f
		
	event_image = { #Egypt/Mesopotamia
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				lepsius_expedition_in_egypt = yes
				lepsius_expedition_in_mesopotamia = yes
			}
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/oriental/lepsius_oriental_bazar.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #Greece
		trigger = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_greece = yes
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/greece/lepsius_plaka2.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #South America
		trigger = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_south_america = yes
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/south_america/lepsius_south_america_market.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/middleeast/jungle_expedition"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
	}
		
	option = { #What a nice surprise!
		name = lepsius.220.g
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
					has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
					has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_experienced
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 3 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
					has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_famous
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 5 }
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = cautious
							has_trait = romantic
						}
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { #Romantic writes diary
					id = lepsius.230
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = innovative
							has_trait = meticulous
						}
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { #Innovative writes scientific paper
					id = lepsius.240
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = reckless
							has_trait = wrathful
							has_trait = cruel
						}
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { #Tavern fight
					id = lepsius.250
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = charismatic
							has_trait = tactful
							has_trait = brave
						}
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { #Appreciation
					id = lepsius.260
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
						has_trait = hedonist
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { #Ice cream and Lemonade
					id = lepsius.270
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = basic_diplomat
							has_trait = experienced_diplomat

						}
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { #An audience
					id = lepsius.280
					days = { 7 14 }

			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:lepsius_military_attache = {

							has_trait = resupply_commander
							has_trait = expert_artillery_commander

#Lepsius 230: Romantic writes diary

lepsius.230 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.230.t
	desc = lepsius.230.d

	flavor = lepsius.230.f
		
	event_image = { #Egypt/Mesopotamia
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				lepsius_expedition_in_egypt = yes
				lepsius_expedition_in_mesopotamia = yes
			}
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/oriental/lepsius_oriental_diary.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #Greece
		trigger = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_greece = yes
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/greece/lepsius_greece_diary.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #South America
		trigger = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_south_america = yes
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lepsius_writer.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/middleeast/jungle_expedition"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
	}
		
	option = { #A personal diary
		name = lepsius.230.g
		scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_writing_a_diary_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = innovative
							has_trait = meticulous
						}
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { #Innovative writes scientific paper
					id = lepsius.240
					days = { 7 14 }
				}

						OR = {
							has_trait = reckless
							has_trait = wrathful
							has_trait = cruel
						}
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { #Tavern fight
					id = lepsius.250
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}

				limit = {
					scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = charismatic
							has_trait = tactful
							has_trait = brave
						}
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { #Appreciation
					id = lepsius.260
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
						has_trait = hedonist
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { #Ice cream and Lemonade
					id = lepsius.270
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = basic_diplomat
							has_trait = experienced_diplomat

						}
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { #An audience
					id = lepsius.280
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = resupply_commander
							has_trait = expert_artillery_commander
							has_trait = expert_offensive_planner
							has_trait = expert_defensive_strategist
						}
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { #Attaché 
					id = lepsius.290
					days = { 10 20 }

			}
			else = {

					days = { 30 40 }
					popup = yes

		}

					id = lepsius.270
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = basic_diplomat
							has_trait = experienced_diplomat
							has_trait = masterful_diplomat
						}
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { #An audience
					id = lepsius.280
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = resupply_commander
							has_trait = expert_artillery_commander
							has_trait = expert_offensive_planner
							has_trait = expert_defensive_strategist
						}
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { #Attaché 
					id = lepsius.290
					days = { 10 20 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				trigger_event = { #Expedition starts
					id = lepsius.300
					days = { 30 40 }
					popup = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
					has_trait = masterful_diplomat
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 2 }
		}
	}

	after = {

					}

					id = lepsius.290
					days = { 10 20 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				trigger_event = { #Expedition starts
					id = lepsius.300
					days = { 30 40 }
					popup = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 300: The Adventure begins

lepsius.300 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.300.t
	desc = lepsius.300.d

	flavor = lepsius.300.f
		
	event_image = { #Egypt
		trigger = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_egypt = yes
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/egypt/lepsius_egypt_expedition_begins.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #Mesopotamia
		trigger = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_mesopotamia = yes
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/mesopotamia/lepsius_mesopotamia_expedition_begins.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #Greece
		trigger = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_greece = yes
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/greece/lepsius_greece_athens_panorama.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #Yucatan
		trigger = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_yucatan_expedition_modifier
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/yucatan/lepsius_yucatan_expedition_begins.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #Peru
		trigger = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_peru_expedition_modifier
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/peru/lepsius_peru_expedition_begins.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/middleeast/jungle_expedition"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
	}

	option = { #Let's go!
		name = lepsius.300.g
		if = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_expedition_in_egypt = yes
			}
			add_journal_entry = {
				type = je_lepsius_archaeological_expedition_egypt
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_expedition_in_mesopotamia = yes
			}
			add_journal_entry = {
				type = je_lepsius_archaeological_expedition_mesopotamia
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_expedition_in_greece = yes
			}
			add_journal_entry = {
				type = je_lepsius_archaeological_expedition_greece
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_expedition_in_south_america = yes
			}
			add_journal_entry = {
				type = je_lepsius_archaeological_expedition_south_america
			}
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 310: The Adventure ends

lepsius.310 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.310.t
	desc = lepsius.310.d
	flavor = lepsius.310.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/egypt/lepsius_egypt_franco_tuscan_expedition.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_military_attache_effect = yes
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_add = yes
	}

	option = { #End expedition and come home
		name = lepsius.310.g
		###Archaeologist Experience ###
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "30"
		}
		###Return Excavation Team###
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = lepsius_add_archaeological_team_tt
			change_variable = {
 				name = lepsius_excavation_teams
 				add = 1
			}
 		}
		###Give artifacts depending on expedition success###
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_expedition_success >= 1
				NOT = {
					var:lepsius_expedition_success >= 5
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_expedition_success >= 5
				NOT = {
					var:lepsius_expedition_success >= 9
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 3 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_expedition_success >= 9
				NOT = {
					var:lepsius_expedition_success >= 13
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 5 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_expedition_success >= 13
				NOT = {
					var:lepsius_expedition_success >= 17
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 7 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_expedition_success >= 17
			}
			lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 10 }
		}
		###Time in which Expeditions are not allowed
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_variable = lepsius_long_expedition_var
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_had_expedition_modifier
				days = 2190
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_variable = lepsius_medium_expedition_var
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_had_expedition_modifier
				days = 1825
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_variable = lepsius_short_expedition_var
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_had_expedition_modifier
				days = 1460
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.310.h
		default_option = yes
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "30"
		}
		trigger = {
			has_technology_researched = lepsius_early_archaeology_tech
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_upper_egypt_expedition_modifier
					NOT = {
						has_modifier = lepsius_upper_egypt_excavation_modifier
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_lower_egypt_expedition_modifier
					NOT = {
						has_modifier = lepsius_lower_egypt_excavation_modifier
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_babylonia_expedition_modifier
					NOT = {
						has_modifier = lepsius_babylonia_excavation_modifier
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_assyria_expedition_modifier
					NOT = {
						has_modifier = lepsius_assyria_excavation_modifier
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_argolis_expedition_modifier
					NOT = {
						has_modifier = lepsius_argolis_excavation_modifier
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_crete_expedition_modifier
					NOT = {
						has_modifier = lepsius_crete_excavation_modifier
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_yucatan_expedition_modifier
					NOT = {
						has_modifier = lepsius_yucatan_excavation_modifier
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_peru_expedition_modifier
					NOT = {
						has_modifier = lepsius_peru_excavation_modifier
					}
				}
			}
		}
		###Give excavation modifier, excavation team does not return
		custom_tooltip = lepsius_leave_team_for_excavation_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_upper_egypt_expedition_modifier
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_upper_egypt_excavation_modifier
				multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_lower_egypt_expedition_modifier
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_lower_egypt_excavation_modifier
				multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_babylonia_expedition_modifier
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_babylonia_excavation_modifier
				multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_assyria_expedition_modifier
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_assyria_excavation_modifier
				multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
			}	
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_argolis_expedition_modifier
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_argolis_excavation_modifier
				multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_crete_expedition_modifier
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_crete_excavation_modifier
				multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_yucatan_expedition_modifier
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_yucatan_excavation_modifier
				multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_peru_expedition_modifier
			}
			add_modifier = lepsius_peru_excavation_modifier
		}
		###Give artifacts depending on expedition success###
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_expedition_success >= 1
				NOT = {
					var:lepsius_expedition_success >= 5
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_expedition_success >= 5
				NOT = {
					var:lepsius_expedition_success >= 9
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 3 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_expedition_success >= 9
				NOT = {
					var:lepsius_expedition_success >= 13
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 5 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_expedition_success >= 13
				NOT = {
					var:lepsius_expedition_success >= 17
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 7 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_expedition_success >= 17
			}
			lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 10 }
		}
		###Time in which Expeditions are not allowed
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_variable = lepsius_long_expedition_var
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_had_expedition_modifier
				days = 1825
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_variable = lepsius_medium_expedition_var
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_had_expedition_modifier
				days = 1460
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_variable = lepsius_short_expedition_var
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_had_expedition_modifier
				days = 1095
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		remove_variable = lepsius_mysterious_guide_var
		remove_variable = lepsius_expedition_artists_var
		remove_variable = lepsius_expedition_scholars_var
		remove_variable = lepsius_expedition_scientists_var
		remove_variable = lepsius_expedition_guards_var
		remove_variable = lepsius_long_expedition_var
		remove_variable = lepsius_medium_expedition_var
		remove_variable = lepsius_short_expedition_var
		remove_modifier = modifier_large_expedition_cost
		remove_modifier = modifier_medium_expedition_cost
		remove_modifier = modifier_small_expedition_cost
		remove_modifier = lepsius_upper_egypt_expedition_modifier
		remove_modifier = lepsius_lower_egypt_expedition_modifier
		remove_modifier = lepsius_babylonia_expedition_modifier
		remove_modifier = lepsius_assyria_expedition_modifier
		remove_modifier = lepsius_argolis_expedition_modifier
		remove_modifier = lepsius_crete_expedition_modifier
		remove_modifier = lepsius_yucatan_expedition_modifier
		remove_modifier = lepsius_peru_expedition_modifier
		scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
			remove_variable = lepsius_military_attache_var
		}
		set_variable = {
            name = lepsius_expedition_success
            value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
            name = lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress
            value = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_writing_a_diary_modifier
				}
			}
			trigger_event = { #Archaeologist finishes Diary
				id = lepsius.311
				days = { 60 90 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_writing_a_scientific_paper_modifier
				}
			}
			trigger_event = { #Archaeologist finishes Scientific paper
				id = lepsius.312
				days = { 60 90 }
			}
		}
		trigger_event = { #Archaeologist returns
			id = lepsius.313
			days = { 10 30 }
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 311: Archaeologist finishs diary

lepsius.311 = {
	type = country_event

    title = lepsius.311.t
	desc = lepsius.311.d

	flavor = lepsius.311.f

	duration = 3
		
	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lepsius_writer.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_diary_writer
		}
	}
		
	option = { #Diary published
		name = lepsius.311.g
		scope:lepsius_diary_writer = {
			remove_modifier = lepsius_writing_a_diary_modifier
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_expeditional_diary_modifier
				days = 1095
			}
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 313: Archaeologist returns (and may get new trait)

lepsius.313 = {
	type = country_event

    title = lepsius.313.t
	desc = lepsius.313.d

	flavor = lepsius.313.f

	duration = 3
		
	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:lepsius_relaxing_archaeologist

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_relaxing_archaeologist
		}
	}
		
	option = { #Welcome back
		name = lepsius.313.g
		lepsius_update_exhibition_effect = yes
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
		}
	}
}

#Events with effect on expedition success

#Lepsius 401: Bedouin Raid/Kurdish Raid

lepsius.401 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					lepsius_expedition_in_egypt = yes
					has_modifier = lepsius_babylonia_expedition_modifier
				}
			}
			desc = lepsius.401.t_bedouin
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_assyria_expedition_modifier
			}
			desc = lepsius.401.t_kurdish
		}
	}

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = { #Egypt/Babylonia
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					lepsius_expedition_in_egypt = yes
					has_modifier = lepsius_babylonia_expedition_modifier
				}
			}
			desc = lepsius.401.f_bedouin
		}
		triggered_desc = { #Assyria
			trigger = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_assyria_expedition_modifier
			}
			desc = lepsius.401.f_kurdish
		}
	}

	duration = 2
		
	event_image = { #Egypt/Babylonia
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				lepsius_expedition_in_egypt = yes
				has_modifier = lepsius_babylonia_expedition_modifier
			}
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/oriental/lepsius_oriental_bedouin_raid.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #Assyria
		trigger = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_assyria_expedition_modifier
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/mesopotamia/lepsius_mesopotamia_kurdish_raid.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
	}
		
	option = { #Do something
		name = lepsius.401.g
		add_treasury = -10000
		scope:lepsius_arrival_state = {
			owner = {
				change_relations = {
					country = ROOT 
					value = -10
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Do nothing
		name = lepsius.401.h
		add_treasury = -5000
		lepsius_expedition_success_small_sub = yes
	}
	option = { #If province is owned
		name = lepsius.401.i
		trigger = {
			scope:lepsius_arrival_state = {
				owner = ROOT
			}
		}
		add_treasury = -5000
		lepsius_expedition_success_small_add = yes
	}
	option = { #GUARDS!
		name = lepsius.401.j
		trigger = {
			has_variable = lepsius_expedition_guards_var
		}
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = lepsius.534.tt
		lepsius_expedition_success_small_add = yes
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 402: Desert Storm/Tropical Storm

lepsius.402 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				lepsius_expedition_in_egypt = yes
			}
			desc = lepsius.402.t_desert
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_yucatan_expedition_modifier
			}
			desc = lepsius.402.t_tropical
		}
	}
		
	desc = lepsius.402.d

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = { #Egypt
			trigger = {
				lepsius_expedition_in_egypt = yes
			}
			desc = lepsius.402.f_desert
		}
		triggered_desc = { #Yucatán
			trigger = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_yucatan_expedition_modifier
			}
			desc = lepsius.402.f_tropical
		}
	}

	duration = 2
		
	event_image = { #Egypt
		trigger = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_egypt = yes
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/egypt/lepsius_egypt_desert_storm.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #Assyria
		trigger = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_yucatan_expedition_modifier
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/yucatan/lepsius_yucatan_tropical_storm.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
	}
		
	option = { #Won't stop us
		name = lepsius.402.g
		random_list = {
			65 = { lepsius_expedition_success_medium_sub = yes }
			35 = { lepsius_expedition_success_medium_add = yes }
		}
	}
	option = { #Too dangerous
		name = lepsius.402.h
		lepsius_expedition_success_small_sub = yes
		default_option = yes
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 403: Fog in the Andes

lepsius.403 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.403.t
		
	desc = lepsius.403.d

	flavor = lepsius.403.f

	duration = 2

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/peru/lepsius_peru_andes.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
		has_modifier = lepsius_peru_expedition_modifier
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_military_attache_effect = yes
		ig:ig_armed_forces = {
			save_scope_as = army_ig
		}
	}
		
	option = { #He should be relieved of his duties.
		name = lepsius.403.g
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_expedition_success_small_add = yes
		scope:army_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_insulted_military_modifier
				days = 730
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #He did a good job.
		name = lepsius.403.h
		lepsius_expedition_success_small_sub = yes
		scope:army_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_praised_military_modifier
				days = 365
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
		}
	}
}

		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_peru_expedition_modifier
			}
			desc = lepsius.404.t_peru
		}
	}
		
	desc = lepsius.404.d

				lepsius_expedition_in_greece = yes

		}
		triggered_desc = { #Peru
			trigger = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_peru_expedition_modifier
			}
			desc = lepsius.404.f_peru
		}
	}

	duration = 2

		}

		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/peru/lepsius_peru_andes.dds"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_greece = yes
			has_modifier = lepsius_peru_excavation_modifier
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
	}
		
	option = { #Rebuild the bridge
		name = lepsius.404.g
		lepsius_expedition_success_medium_add = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_small_expedition_cost
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
			days = 365
		}
	}
	option = { #Find another way
		name = lepsius.404.h
		lepsius_expedition_success_small_sub = yes
		default_option = yes
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 405: Bad Roads in Mesopotamia/Yucatán

lepsius.405 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				lepsius_expedition_in_mesopotamia = yes
			}
			desc = lepsius.405.t_mesopotamia
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_yucatan_expedition_modifier
			}
			desc = lepsius.405.t_yucatan
		}
	}
		
	desc = lepsius.405.d

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = { #Mesopotamia
			trigger = {
				lepsius_expedition_in_mesopotamia = yes
			}
			desc = lepsius.405.f_mesopotamia
		}
		triggered_desc = { #Yucatán
			trigger = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_yucatan_expedition_modifier
			}
			desc = lepsius.405.f_yucatan
		}
	}

	duration = 2
		
	event_image = { #Mesopotamia
		trigger = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_mesopotamia = yes
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/greece/lepsius_greece_mountains.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #Yucatán
		trigger = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_yucatan_expedition_modifier
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/yucatan/lepsius_yucatan_jungle.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
	}
		
	option = { #Try another path.
		name = lepsius.405.g
		random_list = {
			30 = { lepsius_expedition_success_small_add = yes }
			20 = { lepsius_expedition_success_medium_add = yes }
			50 = { lepsius_expedition_success_medium_sub = yes }
		}
	}
	option = { #Invest in new men and beasts of burden to make the journey more enjoyable.
		name = lepsius.405.h
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_expedition_success_small_add = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_small_expedition_cost
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
			days = 365
		}
	}
	option = { #We stay on this road.
		name = lepsius.405.i
		lepsius_expedition_success_small_sub = yes
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 406: Expedition Shipwreck!

lepsius.406 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

	flavor = lepsius.406.f

	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	cooldown = { 
		years = 5
	}

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_military_attache_effect = yes
		ig:ig_armed_forces = {
			save_scope_as = army_ig
		}
	}
		
	option = { #He should be relieved of his duties.
		name = lepsius.406.g
		add_treasury = -5000
		scope:army_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_insulted_military_modifier
				days = 1095
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Let's pretend nothing happened.
		name = lepsius.406.h
		add_treasury = -5000
		lepsius_expedition_success_small_sub = yes
		default_option = yes
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 408: Nazar Amulet

lepsius.408 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.408.t
		
	desc = lepsius.408.d

	flavor = lepsius.408.f

	duration = 2

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/mesopotamia/lepsius_mesopotamia_evil_eye.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	cooldown = { 
		years = 4
	}

	trigger = {
		scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_nazar_amulet_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
	}
		
	option = { #Buy the amulet
		name = lepsius.408.g
		lepsius_expedition_success_small_add = yes
		scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
			add_modifier = lepsius_nazar_amulet_modifier
		}
	}
	option = { #This superstition contradicts every scientific conviction!
		name = lepsius.408.h
		lepsius_expedition_success_small_sub = yes
		default_option = yes
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
		}
	}
}

	option = { #He'll be ours
		name = lepsius.410.j
		trigger = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_peru_expedition_modifier
			scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_famous
					has_trait = explorer
				}
			}
		}
		lepsius_expedition_success_small_add = yes
		lepsius_small_add_technology = yes
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
		}
	}
}

	}

	event_image = { #Greece
		trigger = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_greece = yes
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/greece/lepsius_greece_temple_ruins.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #South America
		trigger = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_south_america = yes
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/yucatan/lepsius_yucatan_plate6_palenque.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	cooldown = { 
		years = 4
	}

	trigger = {
		any_scope_character = {
			has_variable = lepsius_military_attache_var #military_attaché may be killed in assyria
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_military_attache_effect = yes
		ig:ig_armed_forces = {
			save_scope_as = army_ig
		}
	}
		
	option = { #Reward and follow him!
		name = lepsius.419.g
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_expedition_success_small_add = yes
		add_treasury = -5000
		scope:army_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_favor_military_modifier
				days = 1095
			}
		}

	}
	option = { #Let's not make him more important than he is.
		name = lepsius.419.h
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
		}
	}
}

    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.421.t

	flavor = lepsius.421.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/egypt/lepsius_egypt_thebes_ruins.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	cooldown = { 
		years = 4
	}

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
	}

	option = { #He may keep the artifact.
		name = lepsius.421.g
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_expedition_success_small_add = yes
		scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
			add_modifier = lepsius_scarab_modifier
		}
	}
	option = { #All artefacts found are to be given to a museum - without exception!
		name = lepsius.421.h
		lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 1 }
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			has_variable = lepsius_mysterious_guide_var
			factor = 2
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 422: A Temple in the Sand (Egypt)

lepsius.422 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.422.t
		
    desc = lepsius.422.d

	flavor = lepsius.422.f

	duration = 2
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/egypt/lepsius_egypt_thebes_east.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
		lepsius_has_clue = no
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
	}

	option = { #In the footsteps of Alexander the Great...
		name = lepsius.422.g
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_game_rule = lepsius_only_historical_rule
			}
		}
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		lepsius_add_alexander_clue = yes
	}

#Lepsius 429: Crystal skull (South America)

lepsius.429 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.429.t
		
    desc = lepsius.429.d

	flavor = lepsius.429.f
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/south_america/lepsius_south_america_crystal_skull.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = lepsius_crystall_skull_var #only once in a game
		}
		OR = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_yucatan_expedition_modifier
			has_modifier = lepsius_yucatan_excavation_modifier
			has_modifier = lepsius_peru_expedition_modifier
			has_modifier = lepsius_peru_excavation_modifier
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
	}

	option = { #We add it to the collection.
		name = lepsius.429.g
		default_option = yes
		set_variable = lepsius_major_artifact_skull_found_var
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_crystall_skull_modifier
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = { }
				50 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = lepsius.430
						years = { 10 20 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Definitely a fake.
		name = lepsius.429.h
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
		}
		set_variable = lepsius_crystall_skull_var #only once in a game
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			has_variable = lepsius_mysterious_guide_var
			factor = 5
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 430: Fake Crystall skull

lepsius.430 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = ROOT

    title = lepsius.430.t
		
    desc = lepsius.430.d

	flavor = lepsius.430.f
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/south_america/lepsius_south_america_crystal_skull.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	option = { #A national disgrace to our archeology!
		name = lepsius.430.g
		remove_modifier = lepsius_crystall_skull_modifier
		remove_variable = lepsius_major_artifact_skull_found_var
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_fake_crystall_skull_modifier
			years = 25
		}
		custom_tooltip = lepsius.430.tt
	}
}

		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/mesopotamia/lepsius_mesopotamia_assyria.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #Greece
		trigger = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_greece = yes
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/greece/lepsius_greece_areopag.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #South America
		trigger = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_south_america = yes
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/yucatan/lepsius_yucatan_plate19_labnah.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	cooldown = { 
		years = 4
	}

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				country_rank = rank_value:great_power
				NOT = { this = ROOT }
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_camp_country
		}
	}

	option = { #We found it, it's ours
		name = lepsius.437.g
		lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 2 }
		scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
			add_trait = bandit
		}
		scope:lepsius_camp_country = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = -15
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Let's share the artifacts
		name = lepsius.437.h
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		scope:lepsius_camp_country = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = -15
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #They are the rightful owners
		name = lepsius.437.j
		change_infamy = -1
		scope:lepsius_camp_country = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = 15
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
		}
	}
}

			40 = { }
			20 = { lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 2 } }
			20 = { lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 3 } }
			20 = { lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 4 } }
		}
	}
	option = { #Barbaric just to think about it.
		name = lepsius.439.h
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_small_add_technology = yes
		lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 1 }
	}

		}

		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/greece/lepsius_greece_cap_sunion.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #South America
		trigger = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_south_america = yes
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/yucatan/lepsius_yucatan_plate7_palenque.dds"
	}

	}

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		random_country = {
			limit = { 
				country_rank = rank_value:insignificant_power
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_broken_piece_country
		}
	}

	option = { #We kindly ask them to do so.
		name = lepsius.440.g
		lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		scope:lepsius_broken_piece_country = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = 10
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			set_owes_obligation_to = {
				country = scope:lepsius_broken_piece_country
				setting = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #The matter is not that important after all.
		name = lepsius.440.h
		default_option = yes
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 443: Quarrel over a crocodile (Egypt, with scientists)

lepsius.443 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.443.t
		
    desc = lepsius.443.d

	flavor = lepsius.443.f

	duration = 2

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/egypt/lepsius_egypt_qurnah.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	cooldown = { 
		years = 4
	}

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_military_attache_effect = yes
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = { 
				is_ruler = yes 
			}
			save_scope_as = ruler
		}
		ig:ig_armed_forces = {
			save_scope_as = army_ig
		}
		ig:ig_intelligentsia = {
			save_scope_as = intelligentsia_ig
		}
	}
	option = { #He is to hand the crocodile over to the researchers.
		name = lepsius.443.g
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_large_add_technology = yes
		scope:army_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_insulted_military_modifier
				days = 1095
			}
		}
		scope:intelligentsia_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_praised_intelligentsia_modifier
				days = 1095
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Long live taxidermism!
		name = lepsius.443.h
		scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
			add_modifier = lepsius_stuffed_crocodile_modifier
		}
		scope:army_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_praised_military_modifier
				days = 1095
			}
		}
		scope:intelligentsia_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_insulted_intelligentsia_modifier
				days = 1095
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #That is indeed a pretty crocodile...
		name = lepsius.443.i
		scope:ruler = {
			add_modifier = lepsius_stuffed_crocodile_modifier
		}
		scope:army_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_insulted_military_modifier
				days = 1095
			}
		}
		scope:intelligentsia_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_insulted_intelligentsia_modifier
				days = 1095
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 445: Piece of the Epic of Gilgamesh (Mesopotamia)

lepsius.445 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.445.t
		
    desc = lepsius.445.d

	flavor = lepsius.445.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/mesopotamia/lepsius_mesopotamia_gilgamesh.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = lepsius_major_artifact_gilgamesh_found_var
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
	}
	option = { #We must find more pieces.
		name = lepsius.445.g
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			var:lepsius_gilgamesh_pieces < 4
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_journal_entry = je_lepsius_epic_of_gilgamesh
				}
			}
			add_journal_entry = {
				type = je_lepsius_epic_of_gilgamesh
			}
		}
		lepsius_add_gilgamesh_pieces = yes
	}
	option = { #More pieces are always welcome.
		name = lepsius.445.h
		trigger = {
			var:lepsius_gilgamesh_pieces = 4
		}
		lepsius_add_gilgamesh_pieces = yes
	}
	option = { #More pieces are always welcome.
		name = lepsius.445.i
		trigger = {
			var:lepsius_gilgamesh_pieces > 4
		}
		lepsius_add_gilgamesh_pieces = yes
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
		}
	}
}
