		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/peru/lepsius_peru_antiquities.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_peru_expedition_modifier
			has_modifier = lepsius_peru_excavation_modifier
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
	}
	option = { #Unpleasent, but valuable.
		name = lepsius.450.g
		lepsius_medium_add_technology = yes
		lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 2 }
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
		}
	}

		}

#Lepsius 455: Rival Expedition

lepsius.455 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.455.t
		
    desc = lepsius.455.d

	flavor = lepsius.455.f

	duration = 2

	event_image = { #Egypt
		trigger = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_egypt = yes
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/oriental/lepsius_oriental_rival_expedition.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #Mesopotamia
		trigger = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_mesopotamia = yes
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/oriental/lepsius_oriental_rival_expedition.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #Greece
		trigger = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_greece = yes
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/greece/lepsius_greece_caravan.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #South America
		trigger = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_south_america = yes
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/yucatan/lepsius_yucatan_plate15_uxmala.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		random_country = {
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					country_rank = rank_value:major_power
					country_rank = rank_value:great_power
				}
				NOT = { this = ROOT }
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_rival_expedition_country
		}
	}
	option = { #Help them
		name = lepsius.455.g
		default_option = yes
		add_treasury = -7500
		change_infamy = -2
		lepsius_expedition_success_small_sub = yes
		scope:lepsius_rival_expedition_country = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = 10
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #We help them in exchange for their knowledge
		name = lepsius.455.h
		lepsius_small_add_technology = yes
		lepsius_expedition_success_small_add = yes
		change_infamy = 1
		scope:lepsius_rival_expedition_country = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = -5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Food and help only if they leave their treasure to us.
		name = lepsius.455.i
		lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		change_infamy = 3
		scope:lepsius_rival_expedition_country = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = -10
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
		}
	}
}

#Events based on character traits

#Lepsius 461: Sphinx whispers in the night (Lower Egypt) [for leader]

lepsius.461 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.461.t
		
    desc = lepsius.461.d

	flavor = lepsius.461.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/egypt/lepsius_egypt_sphinx.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	cooldown = { 
		years = 4
	}

	trigger = {
		has_modifier = lepsius_lower_egypt_expedition_modifier
		scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
			OR = {
				has_trait = alcoholic
				has_trait = opium_addiction
				has_trait = cocaine_addiction
				has_trait = psychological_affliction
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
	}
	option = { #This man really needs to rethink his lifestyle.
		name = lepsius.461.g
		scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_whispering_sphinx_modifier
				days = 1095
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			has_variable = lepsius_mysterious_guide_var
			factor = 2
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 467: A forgotten Relic (is christian; becomes pious and gets Relic)

lepsius.467 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.467.t
		
    desc = lepsius.467.d

	flavor = lepsius.467.f

	duration = 2

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/oriental/lepsius_oriental_coptic.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	cooldown = { 
		years = 4
	}

	trigger = {
		scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
			OR = {
				religion = rel:catholic
				religion = rel:orthodox
				religion = rel:oriental_orthodox
			}
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_forgotten_relic_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
	}
	option = { #Did he have a beatific vision?
		name = lepsius.467.g
		lepsius_expedition_success_small_add = yes
		scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
			add_trait = pious
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_forgotten_relic_modifier
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = cruel
				}
				remove_trait = cruel
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = arrogant
				}
				remove_trait = arrogant
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #He should study the relic
		name = lepsius.467.h
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_large_add_technology = yes
		
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			has_variable = lepsius_mysterious_guide_var
			factor = 2
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 468: Attaché robbed artifact (if bandit)

lepsius.468 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.468.t
		
    desc = lepsius.468.d

	flavor = lepsius.468.f

	duration = 2

	event_image = { #Egypt/Mesopotamia
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				lepsius_expedition_in_egypt = yes
				lepsius_expedition_in_mesopotamia = yes
			}
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/oriental/lepsius_oriental_painters.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #Greece
		trigger = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_greece = yes
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/greece/lepsius_greece_the_sea.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #South America
		trigger = {
			lepsius_expedition_in_south_america = yes
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/yucatan/lepsius_yucatan_plate16_kabah.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
		any_scope_character = {
			has_variable = lepsius_military_attache_var #military_attaché may be killed in assyria
			has_trait = bandit
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_military_attache_effect = yes
		ig:ig_armed_forces = {
			save_scope_as = army_ig
		}
	}
	option = { #Keep silent about the matter
		name = lepsius.468.g
	}
	option = { #Handle the matter carefully, but insist that he returns the artifacts.
		name = lepsius.468.h
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 2 }
		scope:army_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_insulted_military_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Publicly expose him and discipline him!
		name = lepsius.468.i
		lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 2 }
		scope:army_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_insulted_military_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
		scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_lost_honor_modifier
				years = 5
			}
			remove_trait = bandit
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 472: A Lost World (Yucatán)

lepsius.472 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.472.t
		
    desc = lepsius.472.d

	flavor = lepsius.472.f
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lostworld/lepsius_lostworld1.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/middleeast/jungle_expedition"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_game_rule = lepsius_only_historical_rule
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = lepsius_discovered_lostworld_var #only once in a game
		}
		has_modifier = lepsius_yucatan_expedition_modifier
		game_date >= 1859.5.22 #Birthday of Arthur Conan Doyle
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
	}

	option = { #Is he saying dinosaurs ate our expedition?!
		name = lepsius.472.g
		add_treasury = -20000
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_eaten_by_dinosaurs_modifier
			days = 1095
		}
		scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
			add_trait = scarred
			set_variable = lepsius_dinosaur_trauma_var
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_lost_honor_modifier
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
			set_variable = lepsius_discovered_lostworld_var #only once in a game
			trigger_event = { 
				id = lepsius.581
				days = 1095
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			has_variable = lepsius_mysterious_guide_var
			factor = 5
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 473: The Diary of Prof. Lidenbrock (Argolis)

lepsius.473 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.473.t
		
    desc = lepsius.473.d

	flavor = lepsius.473.f

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_argolis_expedition_modifier
			has_modifier = lepsius_argolis_excavation_modifier
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = lepsius_found_lidenbrock_diary_var #only once in a game
		}
		scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_museum_lead_scientist_modifier
		}
		game_date >= 1864.11.25 #Journey to the Center of the Earth published
		is_player = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
	}
	option = { #A discovery that will benefit everyone.
		name = lepsius.473.g
		lepsius_large_add_technology = yes
	}
	option = { #The leader should keep and study it.
		name = lepsius.473.h
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_game_rule = lepsius_only_historical_rule
			}
		}
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = lepsius.473.tt
		scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_lidenbrock_diary_modifier
			}
			set_variable = lepsius_journey_coe_var
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.591
				days = { 250 350 }
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
			set_variable = lepsius_found_lidenbrock_diary_var #only once in a game
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			has_variable = lepsius_mysterious_guide_var
			factor = 5
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 501: Tomb of an unknown Pharaoh

lepsius.501 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.501.t
		
    desc = lepsius.501.d

	flavor = lepsius.501.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/egypt/lepsius_egypt_sarcophagus.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	cooldown = { 
		years = 10
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_upper_egypt_expedition_modifier
			has_modifier = lepsius_upper_egypt_excavation_modifier
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = lepsius_narrative_sarcophagus_var #only once in a game
			var:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress >= 4 #will only trigger in the beginning of an expedition
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
	}
	option = { #We don't have time for this.
		name = lepsius.501.g
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_on_archaeological_expedition = yes
			}
			lepsius_expedition_success_medium_add = yes
		}
	}
	option = { #Let our leader investigate further.
		name = lepsius.501.h
		set_variable = lepsius_narrative_sarcophagus_var #only once in a game
		custom_tooltip = lepsius.501.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.502
				days = { 3 7 }
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					lepsius_on_archaeological_expedition = yes
				}
				lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			has_variable = lepsius_mysterious_guide_var
			factor = 50
		}
	}
}

			desc = lepsius.505.d_muscular
		}
	}

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_sarcophagus_archaeology_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.505.f_archaeology
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_sarcophagus_engine_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.505.f_engine
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_sarcophagus_muscular_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.505.f_muscular
		}
	}

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/egypt/lepsius_egypt_sarcophagus.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
	}
	option = { #The splendour of Ancient Egypt ...
		name = lepsius.505.g
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_variable = lepsius_sarcophagus_archaeology_var
				has_variable = lepsius_sarcophagus_muscular_var
			}
		}
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_medium_add_technology = yes
	}
	option = { #Oops
		name = lepsius.505.h
		trigger = {
			has_variable = lepsius_sarcophagus_engine_var
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_archaeological_vandalism_modifier 
			years = 5
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.506
				days = { 3 7 }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 506: A Broken Sarcophagus/A Fine Sarcophagus

lepsius.506 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

	title = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_sarcophagus_archaeology_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.506.t_archaeology
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_sarcophagus_engine_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.506.t_engine
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_sarcophagus_muscular_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.506.t_muscular
		}
	}

	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_sarcophagus_archaeology_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.506.d_archaeology
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_sarcophagus_engine_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.506.d_engine
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_sarcophagus_muscular_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.506.d_muscular
		}
	}

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_sarcophagus_archaeology_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.506.f_archaeology
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_sarcophagus_engine_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.506.f_engine
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_sarcophagus_muscular_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.506.f_muscular
		}
	}

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/egypt/lepsius_egypt_sarcophagus.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
	}
	option = { #The splendour of Ancient Egypt ...
		name = lepsius.506.g
		trigger = {
			has_variable = lepsius_sarcophagus_archaeology_var
		}
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = lepsius_add_archaeological_experience_tt
		lepsius_large_add_technology = yes
		lepsius_add_1_major_egyptian_artifact = yes 
		set_variable = lepsius_major_artifact_sarcophagus_found_var
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "25"
		}
		if = { #Used for the overview of the Archaeologist
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
			}
			var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
				set_variable = lepsius_found_sarcophagus_intact_var
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Move it quickly!
		name = lepsius.506.h
		trigger = {
			has_variable = lepsius_sarcophagus_engine_var
		}
		lepsius_add_1_major_egyptian_artifact = yes 
		set_variable = lepsius_major_artifact_sarcophagus_found_var
		if = { #Used for the overview of the Archaeologist
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
			}
			var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
				set_variable = lepsius_found_sarcophagus_intact_var
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Oops
		name = lepsius.506.i
		trigger = {
			has_variable = lepsius_sarcophagus_muscular_var
		}
		lepsius_medium_add_technology = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_archaeological_vandalism_modifier 
			years = 3
		}
		lepsius_add_x_egyptian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 3 }

		if = { #Used for the overview of the Archaeologist
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
			}
			var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
				set_variable = lepsius_found_sarcophagus_broken_var
			}
		}
	}
}


###RAISE THE FLAG (Lower Egypt)

#Lepsius 511: A Question of Honor

lepsius.511 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.511.t
		
    desc = lepsius.511.d

	flavor = lepsius.511.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/egypt/lepsius_egypt_pyramids.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	cooldown = { 
		years = 5
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_lower_egypt_expedition_modifier
			has_modifier = lepsius_lower_egypt_excavation_modifier
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = lepsius_narrative_pyramids_flag_var #only one flag in a game
			var:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress >= 4 #will only trigger in the beginning of an expedition
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
	}
	option = { #We don't have time vor this.
		name = lepsius.511.g
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_on_archaeological_expedition = yes
			}
			lepsius_expedition_success_medium_add = yes
		}
	}
	option = { #Let our leader investigate further.
		name = lepsius.511.h
		custom_tooltip = lepsius.511.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.512
				days = { 3 7 }
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					lepsius_on_archaeological_expedition = yes
				}
				lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			has_variable = lepsius_mysterious_guide_var
			factor = 50
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 512: Dawn

lepsius.512 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.512.t
		
    desc = lepsius.512.d

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
					has_trait = meticulous
				}
			}
			desc = lepsius.512.f_wine
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
						has_trait = meticulous
					}
				}
			}
			desc = lepsius.512.f_no_wine
		}
	}

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/egypt/lepsius_egypt_pyramids.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
			set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
	}
	option = { #Wine
		name = lepsius.512.g
		trigger = {
			scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
				has_trait = meticulous
			}
		}
		default_option = yes
		set_variable = lepsius_narrative_pyramids_wine_var
	}
	option = { #No wine
		name = lepsius.512.h
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
					has_trait = meticulous
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = lepsius_narrative_pyramids_no_wine_var
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.513
				days = { 3 7 }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 513: First step

lepsius.513 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.513.t
		
    desc = lepsius.513.d

	flavor = lepsius.513.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/egypt/lepsius_egypt_pyramids.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
			set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_military_attache_effect = yes
	}
	option = { #The archaeological leader
		name = lepsius.513.g
		default_option = yes
		random_list = {
			40 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = alcoholic
							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = opium_addiction
							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = senile
							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = wounded
							}
						}
						add = 5
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { 
					id = lepsius.516 #Fail
					days = 3
				}
			}
			60 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = cautious
							}
						}
						add = 5
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = meticulous
							}
						}
						add = 5
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
								has_trait = surveyor
							}
						}
						add = 8
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = ambitious
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = brave
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = persistent
							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = explorer
							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { 
					id = lepsius.514 #Second step
					days = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #The attaché
		name = lepsius.513.h
		random_list = {
			40 = {

					if = {

				}

					}

							scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
								has_trait = wounded
							}
						}
						add = 5
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { 
					id = lepsius.516 #Fail
					days = 3
					popup = yes
				}
			}
			60 = {

							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
								has_trait = explorer
							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { 
					id = lepsius.515 #Third step
					days = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #This place is good enough
		name = lepsius.514.i
		custom_tooltip = lepsius.514.tt
		set_variable = lepsius_narrative_pyramids_flag_var
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_pyramid_flag_low_modifier
			years = 3
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 515: Third step

lepsius.515 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.515.t
		
    desc = lepsius.515.d

	flavor = lepsius.515.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/egypt/lepsius_egypt_pyramids.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
			set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_military_attache_effect = yes
		ig:ig_armed_forces = {
			save_scope_as = army_ig
		}
		ig:ig_intelligentsia = {
			save_scope_as = intelligentsia_ig
		}
	}
	option = { #The archaeological leader
		name = lepsius.513.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:intelligentsia_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_praised_intelligentsia_modifier
				days = 365
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			55 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = alcoholic
							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = opium_addiction
							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = senile
							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = wounded
							}
						}
						add = 5
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { 
					id = lepsius.516 #Fail
					days = 3
				}
			}
			45 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = cautious
							}
						}
						add = 10 #the last bit needs more caution
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = meticulous
							}
						}
						add = 10 #the last bit needs more caution
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
								has_trait = surveyor
							}
						}
						add = 10 #the last bit needs more caution
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = ambitious
							}
						}
						add = 5 #the last bit needs more caution
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = brave
							}
						}
						add = 5 #the last bit needs more caution
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = persistent
							}
						}
						add = 25 #persistance more important than ever
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = explorer
							}
						}
						add = 20 #exploration skill more important
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_experienced
							}
						}
						add = 10 #an experienced archaeologist will do better
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_famous
							}
						}
						add = 15 #an experienced archaeologist will do better
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { 
					id = lepsius.517 #Raise the Flag!
					days = 3
					popup = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #The attaché
		name = lepsius.513.h
		scope:army_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_praised_military_modifier
				days = 365
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			55 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
								has_trait = alcoholic
							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
								has_trait = opium_addiction
							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
								has_trait = senile
							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
								has_trait = wounded
							}
						}
						add = 5
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { 
					id = lepsius.516 #Fail
					days = 3
				}
			}
			45 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
								has_trait = cautious
							}
						}
						add = 10 #the last bit needs more caution

	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_military_attache_effect = yes
	}
	option = { #Embarrasing
		name = lepsius.516.g
		custom_tooltip = lepsius.516.tt
		lepsius_expedition_success_small_sub = yes
		remove_variable = lepsius_narrative_pyramids_wine_var
		remove_variable = lepsius_narrative_pyramids_no_wine_var
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_pyramid_flag_top_modifier
			years = 5
		}
		scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
			add_trait = wounded
		}
		scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
			add_trait = wounded
		}
	}

#Lepsius 517: Raise the Flag!

lepsius.517 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.517.t
		
    desc = lepsius.517.d

	flavor = lepsius.517.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/egypt/lepsius_egypt_pyramids_flag.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_military_attache_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
			}
			var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
				set_variable = lepsius_raised_flag_on_pyramids_var
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Raise the flag of $COUNTRY$! [Wine]
		name = lepsius.517.g
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			has_variable = lepsius_narrative_pyramids_wine_var
		}
		custom_tooltip = lepsius.514.tt
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "25"
		}
		set_variable = lepsius_narrative_pyramids_flag_var
		lepsius_medium_add_technology = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_pyramid_flag_top_wine_modifier
			years = 5
		}
		scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = explorer
				}
				add_trait = brave
			}
			else = {
				add_trait = explorer
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Raise the flag of $COUNTRY$! [No Wine]
		name = lepsius.517.g
		trigger = {
			has_variable = lepsius_narrative_pyramids_no_wine_var
		}
		custom_tooltip = lepsius.514.tt
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "25"
		}
		set_variable = lepsius_narrative_pyramids_flag_var
		lepsius_medium_add_technology = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_pyramid_flag_top_modifier
			years = 5
		}
		scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = explorer
				}
				add_trait = brave
			}
			else = {
				add_trait = explorer
			}
		}
	}
}


###THE ISHTAR GATE

#Lepsius 521: The Ishtar Gate found

lepsius.521 = {
	type = country_event

    title = lepsius.521.t
		
    desc = lepsius.521.d

	flavor = lepsius.521.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/mesopotamia/lepsius_mesopotamia_ishtar_gate.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	cooldown = { 
		years = 5
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_babylonia_expedition_modifier
			has_modifier = lepsius_babylonia_excavation_modifier
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = lepsius_narrative_ishtar_build_var
			var:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress >= 4 #will only trigger in the beginning of an expedition
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
	}
	option = { #Just take some parts. It should stay where it is
		name = lepsius.521.g
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_add_x_minor_artifacts = { AMOUNT = 2 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_on_archaeological_expedition = yes
			}
			lepsius_expedition_success_medium_add = yes
		}
	}
	option = { #It should be transported to $CAPITAL$ and reconstructed
		name = lepsius.521.h
		custom_tooltip = lepsius.521.tt
		set_global_variable = lepsius_narrative_ishtar_build_var #only one country can have this
		set_variable = {
            name = lepsius_ishtar_fragments
            value = 0
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_ishtar_gate_cost_modifier
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
		}
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_ishtar_gate
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = { #first fragments free
				id = lepsius.522
				days = 30
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					lepsius_on_archaeological_expedition = yes
				}
				lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			has_variable = lepsius_mysterious_guide_var
			factor = 50
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 523: Rival has fragments

lepsius.523 = {
	type = country_event

    title = lepsius.523.t
		
    desc = lepsius.523.d

	flavor = lepsius.523.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/mesopotamia/lepsius_mesopotamia_ishtar_bull2.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
		has_modifier = lepsius_babylonia_excavation_modifier
	}

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					country_rank = rank_value:major_power
					country_rank = rank_value:great_power
				}
				NOT = { this = ROOT }
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_rival_ishtar_country
		}
	}

	option = { #We shall probably humble ourselves
		name = lepsius.523.g
		lepsius_add_20k_ishtar_fragments = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_diplomatic_prostration_modifier
			years = 2
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:lepsius_rival_ishtar_country = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = lepsius.529
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Never!
	default_option = yes
		name = lepsius.523.h
	}
}

#Lepsius 530: Ishtar Gate reconstructed

	type = country_event

    title = lepsius.530.t
		
    desc = lepsius.530.d

	flavor = lepsius.530.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/mesopotamia/lepsius_mesopotamia_ishtar_gate_museum.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
		has_modifier = lepsius_babylonia_excavation_modifier
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
			}
			var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
				set_variable = lepsius_reconstructed_ishtar_gate_var
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Magnificient!
		name = lepsius.530.g
		remove_modifier = lepsius_ishtar_gate_cost_modifier
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_ishtar_gate_modifier
		}
	}
}


###THE LAMASSU (Assyria)

#Lepsius 531: The Legend of the Lamassu

lepsius.531 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.531.t
		
    desc = lepsius.531.d

	flavor = lepsius.531.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/mesopotamia/lepsius_mesopotamia_lion_of_nimrud.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	cooldown = { 
		years = 5
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_assyria_expedition_modifier
			has_modifier = lepsius_assyria_excavation_modifier
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = lepsius_major_artifact_lamassu_found_var #only one Lamassu in a game
			var:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress >= 4 #will only trigger in the beginning of an expedition
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
	}
	option = { #We don't have time vor this.
		name = lepsius.531.g
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_on_archaeological_expedition = yes
			}
			lepsius_expedition_success_medium_add = yes
		}
	}
	option = { #Let our leader investigate further.
		name = lepsius.531.h
		custom_tooltip = lepsius.531.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.532
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					lepsius_on_archaeological_expedition = yes
				}
				lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			has_variable = lepsius_mysterious_guide_var
			factor = 50
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 533: Gifts

lepsius.533 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.533.t
		
    desc = lepsius.533.d

	flavor = lepsius.533.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/mesopotamia/lepsius_mesopotamia_kurdish_tent.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
			set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
	}
	option = { #Finest clothes
		name = lepsius.533.g
		default_option = yes
		add_treasury = -10000
		random_list = {
			60 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = grifter
							}
						}
						add = 30
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { 
					id = lepsius.534 #Insulted
					days = 3
				}
			}
			40 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = expensive_tastes
							}
						}
						add = 100
					}
				}
				set_variable = lepsius_kurds_persuaded_var
				trigger_event = { 
					id = lepsius.540 #Persuaded
					days = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Remind them of honor and hospitality
		name = lepsius.533.h
		random_list = {
			55 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = direct
							}

						add = 5
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = imperious
							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = arrogant
							}
						}
						add = 25
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = bigoted
							}
						}
						add = 25
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = reckless
							}
						}
						add = 25
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { 
					id = lepsius.534 #Insulted
					days = 3
				}
			}
			45 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = cautious
							}
						}
						add = 5
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = pious
							}
						}
						add = 5
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = brave
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = tactful
							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = charismatic
							}
						}
						add = 20
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = basic_diplomat
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = experienced_diplomat
							}
						}
						add = 20
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {

							}
						}

				modifier = {

							}
						}
						add = 100
					}

					}

				trigger_event = { 
					id = lepsius.540 #Persuaded
					days = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Kotau
		name = lepsius.533.i
		change_infamy = -1
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_adjacent_to_country = THIS
			}
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = -10
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_diplomatic_prostration_modifier
			years = 10
		}
		scope:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_leader = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_lost_honor_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			45 = {

					days = 3
				}
			}

				trigger_event = {

					days = 3
				}
			}

		custom_tooltip = lepsius.534.tt

			id = lepsius.540 #Victory!
			days = 3
			popup = yes
		}
	}
	option = { #DEFEND
		name = lepsius.534.h
		random_list = {
			65 = {
				trigger_event = { 
					id = lepsius.539 #A noble death
					days = 3
				}
			}

				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
								has_trait = brave
							}
						}
						add = 5
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
								has_trait = charismatic
							}
						}
						add = 5
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
								has_trait = experienced_artillery_commander
							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
								has_trait = expert_artillery_commander
							}
						}
						add = 25
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
								has_trait = basic_defensive_strategist
							}
						}
						add = 30
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
								has_trait = experienced_defensive_strategist
							}
						}
						add = 40
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
								has_trait = expert_defensive_strategist
							}
						}
						add = 50
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
								has_trait = stalwart_defender
							}
						}
						add = 100
					}
				}
				set_variable = lepsius_kurds_defeated_var
				trigger_event = { 
					id = lepsius.540 #Victory!
					days = 3
					popup = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

		}

#Lepsius 540: The Lamassu

lepsius.540 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.540.t
		
    desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_kurds_persuaded_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.540.d
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_kurds_defeated_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.540.d_victory
		}
	}

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_kurds_persuaded_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.540.f
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_kurds_defeated_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.540.f_victory
		}
	}

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/mesopotamia/lepsius_mesopotamia_lion_of_nimrud.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_military_attache_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
			}
			var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
				set_variable = lepsius_found_lamassu_var
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #It is wonderful!
		name = lepsius.540.g
		set_variable = lepsius_major_artifact_lamassu_found_var #only one Lamassu in a game
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "25"
		}
		lepsius_add_1_major_mesopotamian_artifact = yes 
		scope:lepsius_military_attache = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_trait = mountain_commander
					}
					has_variable = lepsius_kurds_defeated_var
				}
				add_trait = mountain_commander
			}
		}
	}
}


###THE LABYRINTH (Crete)

#Lepsius 551: An archaeological Incident

lepsius.551 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.551.t
		
    desc = lepsius.551.d

	flavor = lepsius.551.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/greece/lepsius_greece_labyrinth.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_crete_expedition_modifier
			has_modifier = lepsius_crete_excavation_modifier
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = lepsius_narrative_labyrinth_var #only once in a game
			var:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress >= 4 #will only trigger in the beginning of an expedition
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
	}
	option = { #What happened to him?
		name = lepsius.551.g
		set_variable = lepsius_narrative_labyrinth_var #only once in game
		custom_tooltip = lepsius.551.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.552
				days = 3
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					lepsius_on_archaeological_expedition = yes
				}
				lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

###THE PYRAMID RIDDLE (Yucatán)

#Lepsius 561: The Myterious Pyramid (Yucatán)

lepsius.561 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.561.t
		
    desc = lepsius.561.d

	flavor = lepsius.561.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/yucatan/lepsius_yucatan_plate22_chichen_itza.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	cooldown = { 
		years = 10
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_yucatan_expedition_modifier
			has_modifier = lepsius_yucatan_excavation_modifier
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = lepsius_narrative_riddle_var #only once in a game
			var:lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress >= 4 #will only trigger in the beginning of an expedition
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
	}
	option = { #We don't have time vor this.
		name = lepsius.561.g
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_on_archaeological_expedition = yes
			}
			lepsius_expedition_success_medium_add = yes
		}
	}
	option = { #Let our leader investigate further.
		name = lepsius.561.h
		set_variable = lepsius_narrative_riddle_var #only once in a game
		custom_tooltip = lepsius.561.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.562
				days = { 2 5 }
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					lepsius_on_archaeological_expedition = yes
				}
				lepsius_archaeological_expedition_progress = yes
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			has_variable = lepsius_mysterious_guide_var
			factor = 50
		}
	}
}

	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = lepsius.562.t

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
			set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
	}
	option = { #Water, the Snake of Kukulkan
		name = lepsius.562.g
		default_option = yes
		set_variable = lepsius_narrative_riddle_wrong_var
	}
	option = { #Air, representing the sky
		name = lepsius.562.h

	}

	}

#Lepsius 565: An archaeological rival/Leaving the Pyramid

lepsius.565 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = scope:lepsius_arrival_state

    title = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = lepsius_narrative_riddle_right_var
					has_variable = lepsius_narrative_riddle_wrong_right_var
				}
			}
			desc = lepsius.565.t_right
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable= lepsius_narrative_riddle_wrong_wrong_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.565.t_wrong
		}
	}

	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = lepsius_narrative_riddle_right_var
					has_variable = lepsius_narrative_riddle_wrong_right_var
				}
			}
			desc = lepsius.565.d_right
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_narrative_riddle_wrong_wrong_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.565.d_wrong
		}
	}

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_narrative_riddle_right_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.565.f_right
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_narrative_riddle_wrong_right_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.565.f_wrong_right
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_narrative_riddle_wrong_wrong_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.565.f_wrong
		}
	}

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/yucatan/lepsius_yucatan_plate22_chichen_itza.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		lepsius_archaeological_expedition_location = yes
		set_archaeological_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		random_rival_country = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeological_rival
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
			}
			var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
				set_variable = lepsius_survived_maya_pyramid_var
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Let's go home
		name = lepsius.565.g
		trigger = {
			has_variable = lepsius_narrative_riddle_right_var
		}
		lepsius_medium_add_technology = yes
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_add_x_precolumbian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
	}
	option = { #Let's go home
		name = lepsius.565.g
		trigger = {
			has_variable = lepsius_narrative_riddle_wrong_right_var
		}
		lepsius_medium_add_technology = yes
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_won_against_arch_rival_modifier
			years = 5
		}
		lepsius_add_x_precolumbian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
	}
	option = { #BELLOC!
		name = lepsius.565.h
		trigger = {
			has_variable = lepsius_narrative_riddle_wrong_wrong_var
		}
		add_treasury = -10000
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_lost_against_arch_rival_modifier
			years = 5
		}
		scope:lepsius_archaeological_rival = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.566
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		lepsius_update_exhibition_effect = yes
	}
}

###THE LOST WORLD###

#Lepsius 581: Return to the Lost World (Yucatán)

lepsius.581 = {
	type = country_event

    title = lepsius.581.t
		
    desc = lepsius.581.d

	flavor = lepsius.581.f
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lostworld/lepsius_lostworld1.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/middleeast/jungle_expedition"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
		has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			has_variable = lepsius_dinosaur_trauma_var
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_lostworld_leader
		}
	}

	option = { #He should restore his honor
		name = lepsius.581.g
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_small_expedition_cost
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_support_for_suicide_mission_modifier
		}
		scope:lepsius_lostworld_leader = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = { 
				id = lepsius.584
				days = { 90 120 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #May he hunt his dinosaurs.
		name = lepsius.581.h
		scope:lepsius_lostworld_leader = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_technology_researched = camera
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = lepsius.582
					days = { 90 120 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				trigger_event = { 
				id = lepsius.583
				days = { 90 120 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Our national interests trump the bruised egos of lousy individuals.
		name = lepsius.581.i
		scope:lepsius_lostworld_leader = {
			add_trait = psychological_affliction
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 582: Disregarded explorer returns triumphant

lepsius.582 = {
	type = country_event

    title = lepsius.582.t
		
    desc = lepsius.582.d

	flavor = lepsius.582.f
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lostworld/lepsius_lostworld2.dds"
	}

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/middleeast/jungle_expedition"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_lostworld_leader
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
			}
			var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
				set_variable = lepsius_photo_evidence_independent_var
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #He ... was right?
		name = lepsius.582.g
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_disregarded_a_hero_modifier
			years = 5
		}
		scope:lepsius_lostworld_leader = {
			remove_modifier = lepsius_lost_honor_modifier
			add_trait = explorer
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 586: Maya presence

lepsius.586 = {
	type = country_event

    title = lepsius.586.t

	flavor = lepsius.586.f
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lostworld/lepsius_lostworld2.dds"

		has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			has_variable = lepsius_dinosaur_trauma_var
		}

		}

					if = {

								has_trait = alcoholic

					}
				}

						add = 15
					}
				}

							scope:lepsius_lostworld_leader = {

							}

					}
				}

								has_trait = meticulous
							}
						}
						add = 5
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_lostworld_leader = {
								has_trait = ambitious
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_lostworld_leader = {
								has_trait = brave
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:lepsius_lostworld_leader = {
								has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_experienced
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}

		has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			has_variable = lepsius_dinosaur_trauma_var
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_lostworld_leader
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
			}
			var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
				set_variable = lepsius_photo_support_var
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Glory to him!
		name = lepsius.589.g
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "25"
		}
		remove_modifier = modifier_small_expedition_cost
		remove_modifier = lepsius_support_for_suicide_mission_modifier
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_supported_a_hero_modifier
			years = 5
		}
		lepsius_update_exhibition_effect = yes
	}
}

							scope:lepsius_journey_coe_leader = {
								has_trait = romantic
							}
						}

					}

				modifier = {

							scope:lepsius_journey_coe_leader = {
								has_trait = persistent
							}
						}
						add = 5
					}

		change_infamy = 5
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_internationally_outlawed_grave_robber_modifier
			years = 5
		}
		scope:lepsius_protest_country = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.703
			}
		}	
		scope:lepsius_protest_country = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = -25
			}
		}	
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_adjacent_to_country = ROOT
			}
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = -10
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.706
				days = { 3 7 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #We will certainly find an amicable agreement.
		name = lepsius.702.h
		change_infamy = 2
		add_treasury = -50000
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_diplomatic_concessions_modifier
			years = 3
		}
		scope:lepsius_protest_country = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.704
			}
		}		
		scope:lepsius_protest_country = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = -10
			}
		}	
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.706
				days = { 3 7 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Donate the artifact as a token of our philanthropy.
		name = lepsius.702.i
		change_infamy = -5
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_internationally_respected_philanthropist
			years = 5
		}
		scope:lepsius_protest_country = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.704
			}
		}	
		scope:lepsius_protest_country = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = 25
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_adjacent_to_country = ROOT
			}
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = 10
			}
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 703: Notification 1

lepsius.703 = {
	type = country_event

    title = lepsius.703.t
		
    desc = lepsius.703.d

	flavor = lepsius.703.f
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lepsius_diplomacy.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_smuggling_major_artifact_var
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_smuggler_country
		}
	}

	option = { #This arrogance is unbelievable!
		name = lepsius.703.g
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_lost_against_arch_rival_modifier
			years = 3
		}
	}
	after = {
		remove_variable = lepsius_protesting_against_smuggle_var
	}
}

#Lepsius 704: Notification 2

lepsius.704 = {
	type = country_event

    title = lepsius.704.t
		
    desc = lepsius.704.d

	flavor = lepsius.704.f
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lepsius_diplomacy.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_smuggling_major_artifact_var
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_smuggler_country
		}
	}

	option = { #Glad they realized they were wrong.
		name = lepsius.704.g
		add_treasury = 50000
		lepsius_add_x_egyptian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		lepsius_add_x_mesopotamian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 1}
		lepsius_add_x_aegean_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		lepsius_add_x_aegean_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 1}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_diplomatic_superiority_modifier
			years = 3
		}
	}
	after = {
		remove_variable = lepsius_protesting_against_smuggle_var
	}
}

#Lepsius 705: Notification 3, not used

#Lepsius 706: Major Artifact arrived!

lepsius.706 = {
	type = country_event

    title = lepsius.706.t
		
    desc = lepsius.706.d

	flavor = lepsius.706.f
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/museum/lepsius_museum_interior.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	option = { #It will be the finest exhibit in our collection.
		name = lepsius.711.g
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_smuggle_tut_var
			}
			lepsius_add_1_major_egyptian_artifact = yes
			set_variable = lepsius_major_artifact_tut_found_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_smuggle_nefertiti_var
			}
			lepsius_add_1_major_egyptian_artifact = yes
			set_variable = lepsius_major_artifact_nefertiti_found_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_smuggle_narmer_var
			}
			lepsius_add_1_major_egyptian_artifact = yes
			set_variable = lepsius_major_artifact_narmer_found_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_smuggle_sargon_var
			}
			lepsius_add_1_major_mesopotamian_artifact = yes
			set_variable = lepsius_major_artifact_sargon_found_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_smuggle_meskalamdug_var
			}
			lepsius_add_1_major_mesopotamian_artifact = yes
			set_variable = lepsius_major_artifact_meskalamdug_found_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_smuggle_agamemnon_var
			}
			lepsius_add_1_major_aegean_artifact = yes
			set_variable = lepsius_major_artifact_agamemnon_found_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_smuggle_diskos_var
			}
			lepsius_add_1_major_aegean_artifact = yes
			set_variable = lepsius_major_artifact_diskos_found_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_smuggle_snake_var
			}
			lepsius_add_1_major_aegean_artifact = yes
			set_variable = lepsius_major_artifact_snake_found_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_smuggle_pakal_var
			}
			lepsius_add_1_major_precolumbian_artifact = yes
			set_variable = lepsius_major_artifact_pakal_found_var
		}
	}
	after = {
		remove_variable = lepsius_smuggling_major_artifact_var
		remove_variable = lepsius_smuggle_tut_var
		remove_variable = lepsius_smuggle_nefertiti_var
		remove_variable = lepsius_smuggle_narmer_var
		remove_variable = lepsius_smuggle_sargon_var
		remove_variable = lepsius_smuggle_meskalamdug_var
		remove_variable = lepsius_smuggle_agamemnon_var
		remove_variable = lepsius_smuggle_diskos_var
		remove_variable = lepsius_smuggle_snake_var
		remove_variable = lepsius_smuggle_pakal_var

		lepsius_update_exhibition_effect = yes
	}
}

######EGYPTIAN ARTIFACTS######

#Lepsius 711: Mask of Tutankhamun

lepsius.711 = {
	type = country_event

    title = lepsius.711.t
		
    desc = lepsius.711.d

	flavor = lepsius.711.f
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/discoveries/lepsius_discoveries_tut.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	option = { #It will be the finest exhibit in our collection.
		name = lepsius.711.g
		trigger = {
			any_scope_state = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_upper_egypt_modifier
			}
		}
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_add_1_major_egyptian_artifact = yes 
		set_variable = lepsius_major_artifact_tut_found_var
	}
	option = { #We should try to get the artifact out of the country safely...
		name = lepsius.711.h
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_scope_state = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_upper_egypt_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = lepsius_smuggling_major_artifact_var
		set_variable = lepsius_smuggle_tut_var
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				85 = {
					random_country = {			
						limit = {
							any_scope_state = {
								has_modifier = lepsius_upper_egypt_modifier
							}
						}
						trigger_event = {
							id = lepsius.701
							days = { 7 14 }
						}
					}
				}
				15 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = lepsius.706
						days = { 7 14 }
					}
				}
			}
		}		
	}
}

				any_scope_state = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_crete_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = lepsius_smuggling_major_artifact_var
		set_variable = lepsius_smuggle_snake_var
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				85 = {
					random_country = {			
						limit = {
							any_scope_state = {
								has_modifier = lepsius_crete_modifier
							}
						}
						trigger_event = {
							id = lepsius.701
							days = { 7 14 }
						}
					}
				}
				15 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = lepsius.706
						days = { 7 14 }
					}
				}
			}
		}		
	}
}

		lepsius_remove_new_archaeologist_effect = yes
		lepsius_update_exhibition_effect = yes
	}

	option = { #The true treassure is Schliemann!
		name = lepsius.743.h
		
		trigger = {
			is_player = yes
		}

		lepsius_set_new_archaeologist_as_archaeologist_effect = yes
	}

	after = {
		set_variable = lepsius_got_priams_treasure_var
	}
}

#Excavations

#Lepsius 801: Excavation Inspection - Site

lepsius.801 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = ROOT

	title = lepsius.801.t
	desc = lepsius.801.d
	flavor = lepsius.801.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_london_center.bk2"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	option = {
		name = lepsius.801.g #Upper Egypt
		trigger = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_upper_egypt_excavation_modifier
			var:lepsius_egyptian_artifact_minor >= 30
			NOT = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_discovery_tut_found_var
			}
		}
		set_variable = lepsius_excavation_inspection_vok_var
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.801.h #Lower Egypt
		trigger = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_lower_egypt_excavation_modifier
			var:lepsius_egyptian_artifact_minor >= 30
			NOT = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_discovery_ship_found_var
			}
		}
		set_variable = lepsius_excavation_inspection_pyr_var
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.801.i #Babylonia
		trigger = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_babylonia_excavation_modifier
			var:lepsius_mesopotamian_artifact_minor >= 30
			NOT = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_discovery_babylon_found_var
			}
		}
		set_variable = lepsius_excavation_inspection_bab_var
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.801.j #Assyria
		trigger = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_assyria_excavation_modifier
			var:lepsius_mesopotamian_artifact_minor >= 30
			NOT = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_discovery_semiramis_found_var
			}
		}
		set_variable = lepsius_excavation_inspection_ass_var
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.801.k #Argolis
		trigger = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_argolis_excavation_modifier
			var:lepsius_aegean_artifact_minor >= 30
			NOT = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_discovery_mycenae_found_var
			}
		}
		set_variable = lepsius_excavation_inspection_arg_var
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.801.l #Yucatán
		trigger = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_yucatan_excavation_modifier
			var:lepsius_precolumbian_artifact_minor >= 30
			NOT = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_discovery_pakal_found_var
			}
		}
		set_variable = lepsius_excavation_inspection_yuc_var
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.801.m #Nevermind
		default_option = yes
		remove_variable = lepsius_inspect_excavation_decision_on
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = lepsius_inspect_excavation_decision_on
				}
				trigger_event = { 
					id = lepsius.802
					days = 7
					popup = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 803: Excavation Inspection - Departure

lepsius.803 = {
	type = country_event
    placement = ROOT

	title = lepsius.803.t
	desc = lepsius.803.d
	flavor = lepsius.803.f

	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:lepsius_archaeological_excavation_leader

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		set_archaeological_excavation_leader_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.803.g 
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_excavation_inspection_vok_var
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_upper_egypt_inspection_modifier
				multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_small
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_excavation_inspection_pyr_var
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_lower_egypt_inspection_modifier
				multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_small
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_excavation_inspection_bab_var
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_babylonia_inspection_modifier
				multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_small
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_excavation_inspection_ass_var
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_assyria_inspection_modifier
				multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_small
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_excavation_inspection_arg_var
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_argolis_inspection_modifier
				multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_small
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_excavation_inspection_yuc_var
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_yucatan_inspection_modifier
				multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_small
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = lepsius_inspect_excavation_decision_on
			remove_variable = lepsius_excavation_inspection_vok_var
			remove_variable = lepsius_excavation_inspection_pyr_var
			remove_variable = lepsius_excavation_inspection_bab_var
			remove_variable = lepsius_excavation_inspection_ass_var
			remove_variable = lepsius_excavation_inspection_arg_var
			remove_variable = lepsius_excavation_inspection_yuc_var
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								scope:lepsius_archaeological_excavation_leader = {
									has_trait = imperious
								}
							}
							add = 15
						}
					}
					trigger_event = { 
						id = lepsius.811 #1 clue
						days = { 300 400 }
					}
				}
				50 = {
					trigger_event = { 
						id = lepsius.812 #2 clues
						days = { 300 400 }
					}
				}
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								scope:lepsius_archaeological_excavation_leader = {
									var:lepsius_archaeologist_experience >= 150
								}
							}
							add = 15
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								scope:lepsius_archaeological_excavation_leader = {
									var:lepsius_archaeologist_experience >= 250
								}
							}
							add = 15
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								scope:lepsius_archaeological_excavation_leader = {
									var:lepsius_archaeologist_experience >= 350
								}
							}
							add = 15
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_modifier = lepsius_archaeological_society_modifier
							}
							add = 10
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_technology_researched = analytical_philosophy
							}
							add = 10
						}
					}
					trigger_event = { 
						id = lepsius.813 #3 clues
						days = { 300 400 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			desc = lepsius.812.f_yuc
		}
	}

	event_image = { #Upper Egypt
		trigger = {

	}

		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/egypt/lepsius_egypt_bigeh.dds"

		remove_modifier = lepsius_lower_egypt_inspection_modifier
		remove_modifier = lepsius_babylonia_inspection_modifier
		remove_modifier = lepsius_assyria_inspection_modifier
		remove_modifier = lepsius_argolis_inspection_modifier
		remove_modifier = lepsius_yucatan_inspection_modifier
	}
}

#Lepsius 901: Discovery of the Tomb of Tutankhamun

lepsius.901 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.901.t
	desc = lepsius.901.d
	flavor = lepsius.901.f

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/discoveries/lepsius_discoveries_tut.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = lepsius_discovery_tut_found_var
		lepsius_archaeological_discovery_add = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
			}
			var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
				set_variable = lepsius_found_tutankhamun_var
			}
		}
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_museum_lead_scientist
		}

	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.901.g
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_discovery_tut_modifier
		}
		lepsius_add_x_egyptian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 10 }
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "50"
		}
		lepsius_update_exhibition_effect = yes
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.711
				days = { 7 21 }
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

lepsius.902 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.901.t

			limit = {

		}

	}
}

#######HISTORICITY OF THE EXODUS######

#Lepsius 1101: Exodus - Invitation

lepsius.1101 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1101.t
	desc = lepsius.1101.d
	flavor = lepsius.1101.f

	duration = 1

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lepsius_exodus_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_yes
		set_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_no
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			set_variable = lepsius_attended_exodus_congress_var
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = lepsius.1101.g # Invite the leading archaeological nations
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					this = ROOT 
				}
				has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
				var:lepsius_total_artifacts >= 10
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.1102
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_egyptian_artifact_minor >= 30
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_experience >= 250
				}
			}
			set_variable = lepsius_congress_lauded_var
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_egyptian_artifact_minor >= 15
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_experience >= 100
				}
			}
			set_variable = lepsius_congress_respected_var
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = lepsius_congress_laughed_var
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = lepsius.1103
			days = { 7 14 }
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = lepsius.1109
			days = 180
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 1102: Exodus - An Invitation

lepsius.1102 = {
	type = country_event

	desc = lepsius.1102.d
	flavor = lepsius.1101.f

		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lepsius_exodus_congress.dds"
	}
