	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_congress_host_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_congress_host_country
		}
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			set_variable = lepsius_attended_exodus_congress_var
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = lepsius.1102.g #We'll come
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_congress_attend_modifier
			years = 5
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_egyptian_artifact_minor >= 30
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_experience >= 250
				}
			}
			set_variable = lepsius_congress_lauded_var
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_egyptian_artifact_minor >= 15
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_experience >= 100
				}
			}
			set_variable = lepsius_congress_respected_var
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = lepsius_congress_laughed_var
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = lepsius.1103
			days = { 7 14 }
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 1103: Exodus - Lauded, Respected, Laughed

lepsius.1103 = {
	type = country_event

	title = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_congress_laughed_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.1103.t_laughed
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_congress_respected_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.1103.t_respected
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_congress_lauded_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.1103.t_lauded
		}
	}

	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_congress_laughed_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.1103.d_laughed
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_congress_respected_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.1103.d_respected
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_congress_lauded_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.1103.d_lauded
		}
	}

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_congress_laughed_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.1103.f_laughed
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_congress_respected_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.1103.f_respected
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_congress_lauded_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.1103.f_lauded
		}
	}

	duration = 2

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lepsius_exodus_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_congress_host_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_congress_host_country
		}
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = lepsius.1103.g #
		trigger = {
			has_variable = lepsius_congress_laughed_var
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_laughed_congress_modifier
			years = 5
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = lepsius.1103.h #
		trigger = {
			has_variable = lepsius_congress_respected_var
		}
		lepsius_small_add_technology = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_respected_congress_modifier
			years = 5
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = lepsius.1103.i #
		trigger = {
			has_variable = lepsius_congress_lauded_var
		}
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_medium_add_technology = yes
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = {
			AMOUNT = "3"
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_lauded_congress_modifier
			years = 5
		}
	}

	after = {
		remove_variable = lepsius_congress_laughed_var
		remove_variable = lepsius_congress_respected_var
		remove_variable = lepsius_congress_lauded_var
		trigger_event = {
			id = lepsius.1104
			days = { 7 14 }
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 1104: Exodus - Historical merit or invention?

lepsius.1104 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1104.t
	desc = lepsius.1104.d
	flavor = lepsius.1104.f

	duration = 2

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lepsius_exodus_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
				NOT = {
					this = ROOT
				}
			}
			var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
				save_scope_as = lepsius_bible_defender_scope
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
				NOT = {
					this = ROOT
				}
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					NOT = {
						this = scope:lepsius_bible_defender_scope
					}
				}
			}
			var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
				save_scope_as = lepsius_bible_attacker_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = lepsius.1104.g #The Bible has some historical value as secondary source
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_famous
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_exodus_yes
				add = 3
			}
			custom_tooltip = lepsius_conference_triple_vote_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_experienced
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_exodus_yes
				add = 2
			}
			custom_tooltip = lepsius_conference_double_vote_tt
		}
		else = {
			change_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_exodus_yes
				add = 1
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_historical_critical_school_modifier
			years = 25
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = { #State Church or Freedom of Conscience
				trigger = {
					religion = {
						has_discrimination_trait = christian
					}
					OR = {
						has_law = law_type:law_state_religion
						has_law = law_type:law_freedom_of_conscience
					}
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Pious Archaeologist
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
						has_trait = pious
						OR = {
							has_religion = catholic
							has_religion = orthodox
							has_religion = oriental_orthodox
							has_religion = protestant
							has_religion = jewish
						}
					}
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Powerful Clergy
				trigger = {
					ig:ig_devout = {
						is_powerful = yes
					}
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Humanities scholars tend to differentiate to the point where the thesis dissolves itself
				trigger = {
					has_technology_researched = lepsius_early_archaeology_tech
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Sweet spot for artifacts
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_egyptian_artifact_minor >= 15
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Sweet spot for artifacts
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_egyptian_artifact_minor >= 20
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Sweet spot for artifacts
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_egyptian_artifact_minor <= 25
				}
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = lepsius.1104.h #The Bible has no historical value at all
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_famous
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_exodus_no
				add = 3
			}
			custom_tooltip = lepsius_conference_triple_vote_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_experienced
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_exodus_no
				add = 2
			}
			custom_tooltip = lepsius_conference_double_vote_tt
		}
		else = {
			change_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_exodus_no
				add = 1
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_historical_materialistic_school_modifier
			years = 25
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				is_incorporated = yes
			}
			convert_population = {
				target = rel:atheist
				value = 0.05
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = { #Total Seperation or Atheism
				trigger = {
					religion = {
						has_discrimination_trait = christian
					}
					OR = {
						has_law = law_type:law_total_separation
						has_law = law_type:law_state_atheism
					}
				}
				add = 1
			}	
			modifier = { #Atheist Archaeologist
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
						has_ideology = ideology:ideology_anti_clerical
					}
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Powerless Clergy
				trigger = {
					ig:ig_devout = {
						is_marginal = yes
					}
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Scientists sometimes tend to be a little too convinced of their theories when the system is confirmed all too often
				trigger = {
					has_technology_researched = dubois_theory_of_evolution_tech
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Too few artifacts: Dunning-Krueger
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_egyptian_artifact_minor < 15
				}
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = { #Too many artifacts: Scepticist
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_egyptian_artifact_minor > 40
				}
				add = 3
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = lepsius.1105
					days = { 14 21 }
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = lepsius.1106
					days = { 14 21 }
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = lepsius.1107
					days = { 14 21 }
				}
			}

			1 = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = lepsius.1108
					days = { 14 21 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 1109: Exodus - Decision for Host

lepsius.1109 = {
	type = country_event

	title = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_merit
			}
			desc = lepsius.1109.t_merit
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_invention
			}
			desc = lepsius.1109.t_invention
		}
	}

	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_merit
			}
			desc = lepsius.1109.d_merit
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_invention
			}
			desc = lepsius.1109.d_invention
		}
	}

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_merit
			}
			desc = lepsius.1109.f_merit
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_invention
			}
			desc = lepsius.1109.f_invention
		}
	}

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lepsius_exodus_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_congress_host_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_congress_host_country
		}
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				global_var:lepsius_exodus_yes > global_var:lepsius_exodus_no
			}
			set_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_merit
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				global_var:lepsius_exodus_yes = global_var:lepsius_exodus_no
			}
			set_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_merit
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				global_var:lepsius_exodus_yes < global_var:lepsius_exodus_no
			}
			set_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_invention
		}
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_merit
		}
		name = lepsius.1109.g #You have to classify and interpret the texts correctly.
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_large_add_technology = yes
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "15"
		}
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_invention
			OR = {
				country_has_state_religion = rel:catholic
				country_has_state_religion = rel:orthodox
				country_has_state_religion = rel:oriental_orthodox
				country_has_state_religion = rel:protestant
				country_has_state_religion = rel:jewish
			}
		}
		name = lepsius.1109.h #The Bible is a useless storybook.
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "15"
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				is_incorporated = yes
			}
			convert_population = {
				target = rel:atheist
				value = 0.03
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_invention
			NOR = {
				country_has_state_religion = rel:catholic
				country_has_state_religion = rel:orthodox
				country_has_state_religion = rel:oriental_orthodox
				country_has_state_religion = rel:protestant
				country_has_state_religion = rel:jewish
			}
		}
		name = lepsius.1109.i #We already knew this beforehand.
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "15"
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_the_bible_is_a_lie_modifier
			years = 5
		}
	}

	after = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					this = ROOT 
				}
				has_modifier = lepsius_congress_attend_modifier
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.1110
				popup = yes
			}
		}
		remove_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_yes
		remove_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_no
	}
}

#Lepsius 1110: Exodus - Decision for Others

lepsius.1110 = {
	type = country_event

	title = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_merit
			}
			desc = lepsius.1109.t_merit
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_invention
			}
			desc = lepsius.1109.t_invention
		}
	}

	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_merit
			}
			desc = lepsius.1109.d_merit
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_invention
			}
			desc = lepsius.1109.d_invention
		}
	}

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_merit
			}
			desc = lepsius.1109.f_merit
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_invention
			}
			desc = lepsius.1109.f_invention
		}
	}

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lepsius_exodus_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_congress_host_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_congress_host_country
		}
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_merit
		}
		name = lepsius.1109.g #You have to classify and interpret the texts correctly.
		default_option = yes
		remove_modifier = lepsius_congress_attend_modifier
		lepsius_large_add_technology = yes
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "15"
		}
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_invention
			OR = {
				country_has_state_religion = rel:catholic
				country_has_state_religion = rel:orthodox
				country_has_state_religion = rel:oriental_orthodox
				country_has_state_religion = rel:protestant
				country_has_state_religion = rel:jewish
			}
		}
		name = lepsius.1109.h #The Bible is a useless storybook.
		remove_modifier = lepsius_congress_attend_modifier
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "15"
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				is_incorporated = yes
			}
			convert_population = {
				target = rel:atheist
				value = 0.03
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = lepsius_exodus_invention
			NOR = {
				country_has_state_religion = rel:catholic
				country_has_state_religion = rel:orthodox
				country_has_state_religion = rel:oriental_orthodox
				country_has_state_religion = rel:protestant
				country_has_state_religion = rel:jewish
			}
		}
		name = lepsius.1109.i #We already knew this beforehand.
		remove_modifier = lepsius_congress_attend_modifier
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "15"
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_the_bible_is_a_lie_modifier
			years = 5
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

######THE RISE OF CIVILIZATION######

#Lepsius 1111: Civilization - Invitation

lepsius.1111 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1111.t
	desc = lepsius.1111.d
	flavor = lepsius.1111.f

	duration = 1

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lepsius_civilization_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = lepsius_babylon_yes
		set_global_variable = lepsius_babylon_no
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			set_variable = lepsius_attended_civilization_congress_var
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = lepsius.1101.g # Invite the leading archaeological nations
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					this = ROOT 
				}
				has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
				var:lepsius_total_artifacts >= 15
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.1112
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_mesopotamian_artifact_minor >= 30
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_experience >= 250
				}
			}
			set_variable = lepsius_congress_lauded_var
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_mesopotamian_artifact_minor >= 15
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_experience >= 100
				}
			}
			set_variable = lepsius_congress_respected_var
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = lepsius_congress_laughed_var
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = lepsius.1113
			days = { 7 14 }
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = lepsius.1119
			days = 180
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 1112: Civilization - An Invitation

lepsius.1112 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1111.t
	desc = lepsius.1112.d
	flavor = lepsius.1111.f

	duration = 1

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lepsius_civilization_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_congress_host_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_congress_host_country
		}
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			set_variable = lepsius_attended_civilization_congress_var
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = lepsius.1112.g #We'll come
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_congress_attend_modifier
			years = 5
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_mesopotamian_artifact_minor >= 30
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_experience >= 250
				}
			}
			set_variable = lepsius_congress_lauded_var
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_mesopotamian_artifact_minor >= 15
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_experience >= 100
				}
			}
			set_variable = lepsius_congress_respected_var
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = lepsius_congress_laughed_var
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = lepsius.1113
			days = { 7 14 }
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 1113: Civilization - Lauded, Respected, Laughed

lepsius.1113 = {
	type = country_event

	title = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_congress_laughed_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.1103.t_laughed
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_congress_respected_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.1103.t_respected
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_congress_lauded_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.1103.t_lauded
		}
	}

	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_congress_laughed_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.1113.d_laughed
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_congress_respected_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.1113.d_respected
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_congress_lauded_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.1113.d_lauded
		}
	}

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_congress_laughed_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.1103.f_laughed
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_congress_respected_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.1103.f_respected
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = lepsius_congress_lauded_var
			}
			desc = lepsius.1103.f_lauded
		}
	}

	duration = 2

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lepsius_civilization_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_congress_host_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_congress_host_country
		}
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}

		name = lepsius.1103.g #
		trigger = {
			has_variable = lepsius_congress_laughed_var
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_laughed_congress_modifier
			years = 5
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = lepsius.1103.h #
		trigger = {
			has_variable = lepsius_congress_respected_var
		}
		lepsius_small_add_technology = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_respected_congress_modifier
			years = 5
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = lepsius.1103.i #
		trigger = {
			has_variable = lepsius_congress_lauded_var
		}
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_medium_add_technology = yes
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = {
			AMOUNT = "3"
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_lauded_congress_modifier
			years = 5
		}
	}

		remove_variable = lepsius_congress_respected_var
		remove_variable = lepsius_congress_lauded_var
		trigger_event = {
			id = lepsius.1114
			days = { 7 14 }
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 1114: Civilization - Babylon or different roots?

lepsius.1114 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1114.t
	desc = lepsius.1114.d
	flavor = lepsius.1114.f

	duration = 2

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lepsius_civilization_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
				NOT = {
					this = ROOT
				}
			}
			var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
				save_scope_as = lepsius_babylon_defender_scope
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
				NOT = {
					this = ROOT
				}
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					NOT = {
						this = scope:lepsius_babylon_defender_scope
					}
				}
			}
			var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
				save_scope_as = lepsius_babylon_attacker_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = lepsius.1114.g #Babylon is the cradle of civilization.
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_famous
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_babylon_yes
				add = 3
			}
			custom_tooltip = lepsius_conference_triple_vote_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_experienced
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_babylon_yes
				add = 2
			}
			custom_tooltip = lepsius_conference_double_vote_tt
		}
		else = {
			change_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_babylon_yes
				add = 1
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_panbabylonism_modifier
			years = 25
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = { #The decoder of Akkadian will be biased
				trigger = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_decipherment_akkadian_modifier
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = { #The fascination with astronomy was important in the establishment of Panbabylonism
				trigger = {
					has_technology_researched = verrier_astronomy_tech
					var:verrier_astronomical_objects >= 250
					var:verrier_astronomical_objects < 500
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Sweet spot for artifacts
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_mesopotamian_artifact_minor >= 10
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Sweet spot for artifacts
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_mesopotamian_artifact_minor >= 20
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Sweet spot for artifacts
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_mesopotamian_artifact_minor >= 30
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Sweet spot for artifacts
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_mesopotamian_artifact_minor >= 40
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Countries with excavation will profit from this
				trigger = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_babylonia_excavation_modifier
				}
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = { #Countries with excavation will profit from this
				trigger = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_assyria_excavation_modifier
				}
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = { #Interested in Ishtar Gate
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						has_modifier = lepsius_ishtar_gate_cost_modifier
						has_modifier = lepsius_ishtar_gate_modifier
					}
				}
				add = 3
			}
			modifier = { #Interested in Gilgamesh
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_gilgamesh_pieces >= 1
				}
				add = 3
			}
			modifier = { #Major Mesopotamian Artifact
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_mesopotamian_artifact_major >= 1
				}
				add = 3
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = lepsius.1114.h #Civilization arose in several places.
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_famous
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_babylon_no
				add = 3
			}
			custom_tooltip = lepsius_conference_triple_vote_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_experienced
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_babylon_no
				add = 2
			}
			custom_tooltip = lepsius_conference_double_vote_tt
		}
		else = {
			change_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_babylon_no
				add = 1
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_anti_panbabylonism_modifier
			years = 25
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = { #The fascination with astronomy was important in refuting Panbabylonism
				trigger = {
					has_technology_researched = verrier_astronomy_tech
					var:verrier_astronomical_objects >= 500
				}
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = { #More nuanced approach as archeology advances
				trigger = {
					has_technology_researched = lepsius_modern_archaeology_tech
				}
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = { #Sweet spot for artifacts
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_egyptian_artifact_minor >= 40
				}
				add = 4
			}
			modifier = { #Sweet spot for artifacts
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_precolumbian_artifact_minor >= 40
				}
				add = 4
			}
			modifier = { #Sweet spot for artifacts
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_aegean_artifact_minor >= 40
				}
				add = 4
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = lepsius.1115
					days = { 14 21 }
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = lepsius.1116
					days = { 14 21 }
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = lepsius.1117
					days = { 14 21 }
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = lepsius.1118
					days = { 14 21 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				has_modifier = lepsius_congress_host_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_congress_host_country
		}
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
				NOT = {
					this = ROOT
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_foreign_archaeologist_country_scope
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = lepsius.1107.g #Let's improve our relationships
		default_option = yes
		scope:lepsius_foreign_archaeologist_country_scope = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = 15
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = lepsius.1107.h #Let's improve our reputation
		change_infamy = -2
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Lepsius 1119: Civilization - Decision for Host

lepsius.1119 = {
	type = country_event

	title = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_civilization_panbabylonism
			}
			desc = lepsius.1119.t_panbabylonism
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_civilization_antipanbabylonism
			}
			desc = lepsius.1119.t_antipanbabylonism
		}
	}

	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_civilization_panbabylonism
			}
			desc = lepsius.1119.d_panbabylonism
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_civilization_antipanbabylonism
			}
			desc = lepsius.1119.d_antipanbabylonism
		}
	}

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_civilization_panbabylonism
			}
			desc = lepsius.1119.f_panbabylonism
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_civilization_antipanbabylonism
			}
			desc = lepsius.1119.f_antipanbabylonism
		}
	}

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lepsius_civilization_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_congress_host_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_congress_host_country
		}
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				global_var:lepsius_babylon_yes > global_var:lepsius_babylon_no
			}
			set_global_variable = lepsius_civilization_panbabylonism
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				global_var:lepsius_babylon_yes = global_var:lepsius_babylon_no
			}
			set_global_variable = lepsius_civilization_antipanbabylonism
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				global_var:lepsius_babylon_yes < global_var:lepsius_babylon_no
			}
			set_global_variable = lepsius_civilization_antipanbabylonism
		}
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = lepsius_civilization_panbabylonism
		}
		name = lepsius.1119.g #Mesopotamia is the cradle of Civilization
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_medium_add_technology = yes
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "15"
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_panbabylonism_modifier
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_established_panbabylonism_modifier
				years = 10
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_anti_panbabylonism_modifier
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_criticized_panbabylonism_modifier
				years = 10
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = lepsius_civilization_antipanbabylonism
		}
		name = lepsius.1119.h #There were several places where civilization arose independently.
		lepsius_large_add_technology = yes
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "15"
		}
	}

	after = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					this = ROOT 
				}
				has_modifier = lepsius_congress_attend_modifier
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.1120
				popup = yes
			}
		}
		remove_global_variable = lepsius_babylon_yes
		remove_global_variable = lepsius_babylon_no
	}
}

######THE TROY DEBATE######

#Lepsius 1121: Troy - Invitation

lepsius.1121 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1121.t
	desc = lepsius.1121.d
	flavor = lepsius.1121.f

	duration = 1

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lepsius_troy_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = lepsius_troy_yes
		set_global_variable = lepsius_troy_maybe
		set_global_variable = lepsius_troy_no
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			set_variable = lepsius_attended_troy_congress_var
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = lepsius.1121.g # Invite the leading archaeological nations
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					this = ROOT 
				}
				has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
				var:lepsius_total_artifacts >= 25
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.1122
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_aegean_artifact_minor >= 30
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_experience >= 250
				}
			}
			set_variable = lepsius_congress_lauded_var
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_aegean_artifact_minor >= 15
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_experience >= 100
				}
			}
			set_variable = lepsius_congress_respected_var
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = lepsius_congress_laughed_var
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = lepsius.1123
			days = { 7 14 }
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = lepsius.1129
			days = 180
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 1123: Troy - Lauded, Respected, Laughed

				has_variable = lepsius_congress_laughed_var
			}

		}

				has_variable = lepsius_congress_respected_var

		triggered_desc = {

			desc = lepsius.1103.f_respected
		}
		triggered_desc = {

				has_variable = lepsius_congress_lauded_var

			desc = lepsius.1103.f_lauded

			has_variable = lepsius_congress_respected_var

			name = lepsius_respected_congress_modifier

		}
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_medium_add_technology = yes

			id = lepsius.1124
			days = { 7 14 }
		}
	}

#Lepsius 1124: Troy - Did Schliemann really find Troy?

lepsius.1124 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1124.t
	desc = lepsius.1124.d
	flavor = lepsius.1124.f

	duration = 2

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lepsius_troy_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
				NOT = {
					this = ROOT
				}
			}
			var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
				save_scope_as = lepsius_troy_defender_scope
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
				NOT = {
					this = ROOT
				}
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					NOT = {
						this = scope:lepsius_troy_defender_scope
					}
				}
			}
			var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
				save_scope_as = lepsius_troy_attacker_scope
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
				NOT = {
					this = ROOT
				}
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					NOT = {
						this = scope:lepsius_troy_defender_scope
					}
					NOT = {
						this = scope:lepsius_troy_attacker_scope
					}
				}
			}
			var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
				save_scope_as = lepsius_troy_mediator_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = lepsius.1124.g #Schliemann did find Troy.
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_famous
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_troy_yes
				add = 3
			}
			custom_tooltip = lepsius_conference_triple_vote_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_experienced
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_troy_yes
				add = 2
			}
			custom_tooltip = lepsius_conference_double_vote_tt
		}
		else = {
			change_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_troy_yes
				add = 1
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_troy_homeric_modifier
			years = 25
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = { #Schliemann supporter will be biased
				trigger = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_support_schliemann_modifier
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = { #Passionate Archaeologist
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = romantic
							has_trait = brave
						}
					}
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Has some evidence, but not too much
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_aegean_artifact_minor >= 10
					var:lepsius_aegean_artifact_minor < 25
				}
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = { #Countries with excavation will profit from this
				trigger = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_argolis_excavation_modifier
				}
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = { #Major Aegean Artifact
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_aegean_artifact_major >= 1
				}
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = lepsius.1124.h #Schliemann did find "Troy", but the matter is more complicated.
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_famous
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_troy_maybe
				add = 3
			}
			custom_tooltip = lepsius_conference_triple_vote_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_experienced
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_troy_maybe
				add = 2
			}
			custom_tooltip = lepsius_conference_double_vote_tt
		}
		else = {
			change_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_troy_maybe
				add = 1
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_troy_historical_modifier
			years = 25
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = { #More nuanced approach as archeology advances
				trigger = {
					has_technology_researched = lepsius_modern_archaeology_tech
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Pensive Archaeologist
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = meticulous
							has_trait = erudite
							has_trait = cautious
						}
					}
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Has so much evidence that they contradict each other
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_aegean_artifact_minor >= 25
				}
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = { #Countries with excavation will profit from this
				trigger = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_argolis_excavation_modifier
				}
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = { #Major Aegean Artifact
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_aegean_artifact_major >= 1
				}
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = lepsius.1124.i #There is no real evidence that this is really Troy.
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_famous
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_troy_no
				add = 3
			}
			custom_tooltip = lepsius_conference_triple_vote_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_experienced
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_troy_no
				add = 2
			}
			custom_tooltip = lepsius_conference_double_vote_tt
		}
		else = {
			change_global_variable = {
				name = lepsius_troy_no
				add = 1
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_troy_myth_modifier
			years = 25
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = { #Aknowledged Archaeologists will refute Schliemann
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
						has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_famous
					}
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Sceptical Archaeologist
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = reserved
							has_trait = bigoted
							has_trait = arrogant
						}
					}
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Has little evidence
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_aegean_artifact_minor < 10
				}
				add = 2
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = lepsius.1125
					days = { 14 21 }
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = lepsius.1126
					days = { 14 21 }
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = lepsius.1127
					days = { 14 21 }
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = lepsius.1128
					days = { 14 21 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 1125: Troy - Archaeologists among themselves

lepsius.1125 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1105.t
	desc = lepsius.1105.d
	flavor = lepsius.1105.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lepsius_troy_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_congress_host_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_congress_host_country
		}
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_var
				NOT = {
					this = ROOT
				}
			}
			var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
				save_scope_as = lepsius_foreign_archaeologist_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = lepsius.1105.g #Another friend of archaeology!
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "10"
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Lepsius 1129: Troy - Decision for Host

lepsius.1129 = {
	type = country_event

	title = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_troy_homeric
			}
			desc = lepsius.1129.t_homeric
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_troy_historical
			}
			desc = lepsius.1129.t_historical
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_troy_myth
			}
			desc = lepsius.1129.t_myth
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_troy_disputed
			}
			desc = lepsius.1129.t_disputed
		}
	}

	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_troy_homeric
			}
			desc = lepsius.1129.d_homeric
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_troy_historical
			}
			desc = lepsius.1129.d_historical
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_troy_myth
			}
			desc = lepsius.1129.d_myth
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_troy_disputed
			}
			desc = lepsius.1129.d_disputed
		}
	}

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_troy_homeric
			}
			desc = lepsius.1129.f_homeric
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_troy_historical
			}
			desc = lepsius.1129.f_historical
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_troy_myth
			}
			desc = lepsius.1129.f_myth
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_troy_disputed
			}
			desc = lepsius.1129.f_disputed
		}
	}

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lepsius_troy_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_congress_host_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_congress_host_country
		}
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				global_var:lepsius_troy_yes > global_var:lepsius_troy_maybe
				global_var:lepsius_troy_yes > global_var:lepsius_troy_no
			}
			set_global_variable = lepsius_troy_homeric
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				global_var:lepsius_troy_maybe >= global_var:lepsius_troy_yes
				global_var:lepsius_troy_maybe >= global_var:lepsius_troy_no
			}
			set_global_variable = lepsius_troy_historical
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				global_var:lepsius_troy_no > global_var:lepsius_troy_yes
				global_var:lepsius_troy_no > global_var:lepsius_troy_maybe
			}
			set_global_variable = lepsius_troy_myth
		}
		else = {
			set_global_variable = lepsius_troy_disputed
		}
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = lepsius_troy_homeric
		}
		name = lepsius.1129.g #So Schliemann actually found Troy!
		lepsius_medium_add_technology = yes
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "15"
		}
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = lepsius_troy_historical
		}
		name = lepsius.1129.h #Schliemann dug up the wrong Troy, but the location is correct.
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_large_add_technology = yes
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "25"
		}
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = lepsius_troy_myth
		}
		name = lepsius.1129.i #Troy is most likely pure literature.
		lepsius_small_add_technology = yes
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "10"
		}
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = lepsius_troy_disputed
		}
		name = lepsius.1129.j #This entire congress was a complete waste of time!
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "5"
		}
	}

	after = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					this = ROOT 
				}
				has_modifier = lepsius_congress_attend_modifier
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.1130
				popup = yes
			}
		}
		remove_global_variable = lepsius_troy_yes
		remove_global_variable = lepsius_troy_maybe
		remove_global_variable = lepsius_troy_no
	}
}

#Lepsius 1201: Local archaeological site

lepsius.1201 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1201.t
	desc = lepsius.1201.d
	flavor = lepsius.1201.f

	duration = 3

	placement = scope:lepsius_excavation_site

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:lepsius_archaeologist_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				is_homeland_of_country_cultures = owner
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_excavation_site
		}
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1201.g #10 years
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_local_excavation_modifier
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_local_excavation_cost_modifier
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
			years = 10
		}
		scope:lepsius_archaeologist_scope = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
		scope:lepsius_excavation_site= {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_local_excavation_state_modifier
				years = 10
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.1202
				months = 18
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.1203
				years = 10
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1201.h #7 years
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_local_excavation_modifier
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_local_excavation_cost_modifier
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
			years = 7
		}
		scope:lepsius_archaeologist_scope = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
		scope:lepsius_excavation_site= {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_local_excavation_state_modifier
				years = 7
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.1202
				months = 12
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.1203
				years = 7
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1201.i #5 years
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_local_excavation_modifier
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_local_excavation_cost_modifier
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
			years = 5
		}
		scope:lepsius_archaeologist_scope = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
		scope:lepsius_excavation_site= {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_local_excavation_state_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.1202
				months = 6
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.1203
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Lepsius 1202: Archaeologist returns from local archaeological site

lepsius.1202 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1202.t
	desc = lepsius.1202.d
	flavor = lepsius.1202.f

	duration = 3

	placement = scope:lepsius_excavation_site

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:lepsius_archaeologist_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_local_excavation_state_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_excavation_site
		}
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1202.g #Welcome back
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_experience >= 300
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_local_artifacts_effect = {
				AMOUNT = 5
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_experience < 300
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_experience >= 250
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_local_artifacts_effect = {
				AMOUNT = 4
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_experience < 250
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_experience >= 200
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_local_artifacts_effect = {
				AMOUNT = 3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_experience < 200
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_experience >= 100
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_x_local_artifacts_effect = {
				AMOUNT = 2
			}
		}
		else = {
			lepsius_add_x_local_artifacts_effect = {
				AMOUNT = 1
			}
		}
		lepsius_update_exhibition_effect = yes
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "10"
		}
		scope:lepsius_archaeologist_scope = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

######ANTHROPOLOGY######

###Caves###

#Lepsius 1301: Cave found

lepsius.1301 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1301.t
	desc = lepsius.1301.d
	flavor = lepsius.1301.f

	duration = 3

	placement = scope:lepsius_cave_state

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:lepsius_anthropologist_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_anthropology.dds"

	trigger = {
		lepsius_has_active_anthropologist = yes
		any_scope_state = {
			lepsius_has_cave = yes
			lepsius_has_discovered_cave = no
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_has_cave = yes
				lepsius_has_discovered_cave = no
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_cave_state
		}
		var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_anthropologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1301.g #Fascinating
		default_option = yes
		anthropologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = 25
		}
		lepsius_add_x_human_fossils_effect = {
			AMOUNT = 2
		}
		lepsius_change_anthropological_rating = {
			AMOUNT = 2
		}
		scope:lepsius_cave_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = lepsius_cromagnon_cave_var
				}
				state_region = {
					add_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_cromagnon_cave
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = lepsius_neanderthalensis_cave_var
				}
				state_region = {
					add_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_neanderthalensis_cave
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = lepsius_erectus_cave_var
				}
				state_region = {
					add_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_erectus_cave
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = lepsius_australopithecus_cave_var
				}
				state_region = {
					add_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_australopithecus_cave
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = lepsius_paranthropus_cave_var
				}
				state_region = {
					add_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_paranthropus_cave
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Lepsius 1302: Neanderthal (Neanderthaler)

###Identification##

#Lepsius 1311: Human Fossil identified

lepsius.1311 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1311.t
	desc = lepsius.1311.d
	flavor = lepsius.1311.f

	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:lepsius_anthropologist_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_anthropology.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_anthropologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1311.g #Fascinating
		default_option = yes
		anthropologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = 25
		}
		lepsius_change_anthropological_rating = {
			AMOUNT = 5
		}
		scope:lepsius_anthropologist_scope = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_unknown_paranthropus_human_fossil >= 1
			}
			lepsius_identify_paranthropus_fossil_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_unknown_australopithecus_human_fossil >= 1
			}
			lepsius_identify_australopithecus_fossil_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_unknown_erectus_human_fossil >= 1
			}
			lepsius_identify_erectus_fossil_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_unknown_neanderthalensis_human_fossil >= 1
			}
			lepsius_identify_neanderthalensis_fossil_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_unknown_cromagnon_human_fossil >= 1
			}
			lepsius_identify_cromagnon_fossil_effect = yes
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Lepsius 1312: Identification (hidden)

lepsius.1312 = {
	type = country_event
	
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_fossil_identification_progress = yes

		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
					var:lepsius_anthropologist_experience >= 300
				}
			}
			lepsius_fossil_identification_progress = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
					var:lepsius_anthropologist_experience < 300
					var:lepsius_anthropologist_experience >= 200
				}
			}
			lepsius_fossil_identification_progress = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
					var:lepsius_anthropologist_experience < 200
					var:lepsius_anthropologist_experience >= 100
				}
			}
			lepsius_fossil_identification_progress = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
					var:lepsius_anthropologist_experience < 100
					var:lepsius_anthropologist_experience >= 50
				}
			}
			lepsius_fossil_identification_progress = yes
		}
	}
}

###Completion###

#Lepsius 1321: Cro-Magnon complete

lepsius.1321 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1321.t
	desc = lepsius.1321.d
	flavor = lepsius.1321.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/anthropology/lepsius_cromagnon.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_anthropology.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_anthropologist_scope
			set_variable = lepsius_completed_cromagnon_anthropologist_var
		}
		set_variable = lepsius_cromagnon_complete
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1321.g #Fascinating
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = lepsius_cromagnon_complete_tt
		anthropologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_variable = lepsius_cromagnon_systemized
				}
			}
			set_global_variable = lepsius_cromagnon_systemized
			set_variable = lepsius_cromagnon_systemizer
			lepsius_change_anthropological_rating = {
				AMOUNT = 75
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_player = yes
				}
				post_notification = lepsius_cromagnon_systemized_notification
			}
		}
		else = {
			lepsius_change_anthropological_rating = {
				AMOUNT = 35
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

###Historical Discovery###

#Lepsius 1331: Neanderthaler

lepsius.1331 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1331.t
	desc = lepsius.1331.d
	flavor = lepsius.1331.f

	duration = 3

	placement = scope:lepsius_cave_state

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/anthropology/lepsius_neanderthalensis.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_anthropology.dds"

	trigger = {
		game_date >= 1860.1.1
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_RUHR
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = lepsius_neanderthalensis_systemized
		}
		has_game_rule = lepsius_anthropology_historical_rule
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_RUHR
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_cave_state
		}
		set_global_variable = lepsius_neanderthalensis_systemized
		set_variable = lepsius_neanderthalensis_complete
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1321.g #Our ancestors were not as primitive as we thought
		default_option = yes
		dubois_add_fossil_neanderthaler = yes
		set_global_variable = lepsius_neanderthalensis_systemized
		set_variable = lepsius_neanderthalensis_systemizer
		lepsius_change_anthropological_rating = {
			AMOUNT = 75
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			lepsius_add_neanderthalensis_fossil_effect = yes
			lepsius_add_neanderthalensis_fossil_effect = yes
			lepsius_add_neanderthalensis_fossil_effect = yes
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			post_notification = lepsius_neanderthalensis_systemized_notification
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

###Piltdown Fraud###

#Lepsius 1341: Piltdown was a fraud! (hidden)

lepsius.1341 = {
	type = country_event

	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		has_global_variable = lepsius_piltdown_discovered
		any_country = {
			lepsius_has_anthropologist = yes
			var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
				var:lepsius_anthropologist_experience >= 300
			}
			count >= 3
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = lepsius_piltdown_fraud
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = lepsius_piltdown_fraud
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = dubois_fossil_piltdown
				}
				lepsius_has_anthropologist = yes
				var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
					var:lepsius_anthropologist_experience >= 300
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.1342
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_fossil_piltdown
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.1343
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Lepsius 1342: Piltdown was a fraud! (Scientists)

lepsius.1342 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1342.t
	desc = lepsius.1342.d
	flavor = lepsius.1342.f

	duration = 3

	placement = scope:lepsius_cave_state

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/anthropology/lepsius_piltdown.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_anthropology.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1342.g #In the end, serious science wins
		default_option = yes
		var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
			set_variable = lepsius_exposed_piltdown_fraud_var
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_exposed_piltdown_fraud_modifier
			years = 10
		}
		lepsius_change_anthropological_rating = {
			AMOUNT = 15
		}
		anthropologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = 25
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Lepsius 1343: Piltdown was a fraud! (Owner)

lepsius.1343 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1342.t
	desc = lepsius.1342.d
	flavor = lepsius.1343.f

	duration = 3

	placement = scope:lepsius_cave_state

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/anthropology/lepsius_piltdown.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_anthropology.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1343.g #An international embarrassment beyond compare!
		default_option = yes
		remove_variable = dubois_fossil_piltdown
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_piltdown_fraud_modifier
			years = 10
		}
		lepsius_change_anthropological_rating = {
			AMOUNT = -125
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

###Cave Events###

#Lepsius 1401: Cave Examination

lepsius.1401 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1401.t
	desc = lepsius.1401.d
	flavor = lepsius.1401.f

	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:lepsius_anthropologist_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_anthropology.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_anthropologist_scope
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_has_discovered_cave = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_cave_1
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_has_discovered_cave = yes
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_1
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_cave_2
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_has_discovered_cave = yes
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_1
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_2
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_cave_3
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_has_discovered_cave = yes
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_1
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_2
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_3
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_cave_4
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_has_discovered_cave = yes
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_1
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_2
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_3
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_4
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_cave_5
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_has_discovered_cave = yes
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_1
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_2
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_3
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_4
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_5
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_cave_6
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_has_discovered_cave = yes
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_1
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_2
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_3
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_4
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_5
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_6
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_cave_7
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1401.g #Cave State 1
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:lepsius_cave_1
		}
		scope:lepsius_cave_1 = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_cave_examination_state_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1401.h #Cave State 2
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:lepsius_cave_2
		}
		scope:lepsius_cave_2 = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_cave_examination_state_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1401.i #Cave State 3
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:lepsius_cave_3
		}
		scope:lepsius_cave_3 = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_cave_examination_state_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1401.j #Cave State 4
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:lepsius_cave_4
		}
		scope:lepsius_cave_4 = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_cave_examination_state_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1401.k #Cave State 5
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:lepsius_cave_5
		}
		scope:lepsius_cave_5 = {

		}
		scope:lepsius_cave_6 = {

		}

	option = {

		default_option = yes

			years = 5
		}

#Lepsius 1402: Cave Examination finished

lepsius.1402= {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1402.t
	desc = lepsius.1402.d
	flavor = lepsius.1402.f

	duration = 3

	placement = scope:lepsius_cave_site

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:lepsius_anthropologist_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_anthropology.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_set_cave_site = yes
		lepsius_set_cave_leader = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1402.g #Welcome back
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:lepsius_anthropologist_scope = {
					var:lepsius_anthropologist_experience >= 250
				}
			}
			anthropologist_experience_gain_effect = {
				AMOUNT = 25
			}
			lepsius_add_x_local_artifacts_effect = {
				AMOUNT = 6
			}
			lepsius_add_x_human_fossils_effect = {
				AMOUNT = 10
			}
			lepsius_add_cave_bone_effect = yes
			lepsius_change_anthropological_rating = {
				AMOUNT = 15
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				scope:lepsius_anthropologist_scope = {
					var:lepsius_anthropologist_experience < 250
					var:lepsius_anthropologist_experience >= 150
				}
			}
			anthropologist_experience_gain_effect = {
				AMOUNT = 25
			}
			lepsius_add_x_local_artifacts_effect = {
				AMOUNT = 4
			}
			lepsius_add_x_human_fossils_effect = {
				AMOUNT = 7
			}
			lepsius_add_cave_bone_effect = yes
			lepsius_change_anthropological_rating = {
				AMOUNT = 12
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				scope:lepsius_anthropologist_scope = {
					var:lepsius_anthropologist_experience < 150
					var:lepsius_anthropologist_experience >= 75
				}
			}
			anthropologist_experience_gain_effect = {
				AMOUNT = 25
			}
			lepsius_add_x_local_artifacts_effect = {
				AMOUNT = 2
			}
			lepsius_add_x_human_fossils_effect = {
				AMOUNT = 5
			}
			lepsius_add_cave_bone_effect = yes
			lepsius_change_anthropological_rating = {
				AMOUNT = 10
			}
		}
		else = {
			anthropologist_experience_gain_effect = {
				AMOUNT = 25
			}
			lepsius_add_x_local_artifacts_effect = {
				AMOUNT = 1
			}
			lepsius_add_x_human_fossils_effect = {
				AMOUNT = 3
			}
			lepsius_change_anthropological_rating = {
				AMOUNT = 3
			}
		}
		scope:lepsius_anthropologist_scope = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
		}
	}

	after = {
		scope:lepsius_cave_site = {
			remove_modifier = lepsius_cave_examination_state_modifier
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 1412: Strange Bone

lepsius.1412 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1412.t
	desc = lepsius.1412.d
	flavor = lepsius.1412.f

	duration = 3

	placement = scope:lepsius_cave_site

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/anthropology/lepsius_cave.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_anthropology.dds"

	cooldown = { 
		years = 10
	}

	trigger = {
		has_modifier = lepsius_cave_examination_modifier 
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_set_cave_site = yes
		lepsius_set_cave_leader = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1412.g #We will identify it later
		default_option = yes
		scope:lepsius_cave_site = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_cromagnon_cave
				}
				owner = {
					lepsius_add_unknown_cromagnon_fossil_effect = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_neanderthalensis_cave
				}
				owner = {
					lepsius_add_unknown_neanderthalensis_fossil_effect = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_erectus_cave
				}
				owner = {
					lepsius_add_unknown_erectus_fossil_effect = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_australopithecus_cave
				}
				owner = {
					lepsius_add_unknown_australopithecus_fossil_effect = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_paranthropus_cave
				}
				owner = {
					lepsius_add_unknown_paranthropus_fossil_effect = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

###Foreign Anthropologist###

#Lepsius 1421: Foreign Anthropologist does Exploration

lepsius.1421 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1421.t
	desc = lepsius.1421.d
	flavor = lepsius.1421.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/anthropology/lepsius_cave.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_anthropology.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_has_discovered_cave = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_cave_1
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_has_discovered_cave = yes
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_1
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_cave_2
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_has_discovered_cave = yes
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_1
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_2
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_cave_3
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_diplomatic_pact = {
					who = ROOT
					type = anthropological_invitation
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_anthropological_guest
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1421.g #Cave State 1
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:lepsius_cave_1
		}
		scope:lepsius_cave_1 = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_cave_examination_state_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1421.h #Cave State 2
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:lepsius_cave_2
		}
		scope:lepsius_cave_2 = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_cave_examination_state_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1421.i #Cave State 3
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:lepsius_cave_3
		}
		scope:lepsius_cave_3 = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_cave_examination_state_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		trigger_event = {
			id = lepsius.1423
			days = 3
		}
	}
}

	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_erectus_cave
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_australopithecus_cave
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_paranthropus_cave
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_cave_1
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_erectus_cave
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_australopithecus_cave
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_paranthropus_cave
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_1
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_cave_2
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_erectus_cave
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_australopithecus_cave
					has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_paranthropus_cave
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_1
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:lepsius_cave_2
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_cave_3
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1421.g #Cave State 1
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:lepsius_cave_1
		}
		scope:lepsius_cave_1 = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_cave_examination_state_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1421.h #Cave State 2
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:lepsius_cave_2
		}
		scope:lepsius_cave_2 = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_cave_examination_state_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1421.i #Cave State 3
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:lepsius_cave_3
		}
		scope:lepsius_cave_3 = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_cave_examination_state_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		trigger_event = {
			id = lepsius.1423
			days = 3
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 1423: Cave Exploration by Foreigners ends

lepsius.1423 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1423.t
	desc = lepsius.1423.d
	flavor = lepsius.1423.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/anthropology/lepsius_cave.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_anthropology.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_diplomatic_pact = {
					who = ROOT
					type = anthropological_invitation
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_anthropological_guest
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_cave_examination_state_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_cave_site
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1423.g #Welcome back
		default_option = yes
		remove_modifier = lepsius_foreign_anthropological_examination_modifier
		lepsius_add_cave_bone_effect = yes
		lepsius_change_anthropological_rating = {
			AMOUNT = 5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_player = no
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = lepsius_anthropology_invitation_break
				days = 500
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		scope:lepsius_anthropological_guest = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = lepsius.1424
			}
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 1424: Cave Exploration by Foreigners ends (For Anthropologist nation)

lepsius.1424 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1423.t
	desc = lepsius.1424.d
	flavor = lepsius.1423.f

	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:lepsius_anthropologist_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_anthropology.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		lepsius_set_cave_leader = yes
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_diplomatic_pact = {
					who = ROOT
					type = anthropological_invitation
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_anthropological_host
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1423.g #Welcome back
		default_option = yes
		anthropologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = 25
		}
		lepsius_add_x_human_fossils_effect = {
			AMOUNT = 5
		}
		lepsius_change_anthropological_rating = {
			AMOUNT = 10
		}
		var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:lepsius_anthropological_host = {
					any_scope_state = {
						has_modifier = lepsius_cave_examination_state_modifier
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_cromagnon_cave
					}
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_cromagnon_fossil_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:lepsius_anthropological_host = {
					any_scope_state = {
						has_modifier = lepsius_cave_examination_state_modifier
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_neanderthalensis_cave
					}
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_neanderthalensis_fossil_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:lepsius_anthropological_host = {
					any_scope_state = {
						has_modifier = lepsius_cave_examination_state_modifier
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_erectus_cave
					}
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_erectus_fossil_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:lepsius_anthropological_host = {
					any_scope_state = {
						has_modifier = lepsius_cave_examination_state_modifier
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_australopithecus_cave
					}
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_australopithecus_fossil_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:lepsius_anthropological_host = {
					any_scope_state = {
						has_modifier = lepsius_cave_examination_state_modifier
						has_state_trait = lepsius_state_trait_paranthropus_cave
					}
				}
			}
			lepsius_add_paranthropus_fossil_effect = yes
		}
	}

	after = {
		scope:lepsius_anthropological_host = {
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = lepsius_cave_examination_state_modifier
				}
				remove_modifier = lepsius_cave_examination_state_modifier
			}
			remove_diplomatic_pact = {
				country = ROOT
				type = anthropological_invitation
			}
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 1501: Human Evolution

lepsius.1501 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1501.t
	desc = lepsius.1501.d

	flavor = {
		desc = lepsius.1501_human_fossils
		desc = lepsius.1501_total_human_fossils
		desc = lepsius.1501_total_unknown_human_fossils
		desc = lepsius.1501_cromagnon_human_fossils
		desc = lepsius.1501_neanderthalensis_human_fossils
		desc = lepsius.1501_erectus_human_fossils
		desc = lepsius.1501_australopithecus_human_fossils
		desc = lepsius.1501_paranthropus_human_fossils
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_global_variable = lepsius_cromagnon_systemized
					has_global_variable = lepsius_neanderthalensis_systemized
					has_global_variable = lepsius_erectus_systemized
					has_global_variable = lepsius_australopithecus_systemized
					has_global_variable = lepsius_paranthropus_systemized
				}
			}
			desc = lepsius.1501_taxonomy
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_cromagnon_systemized
			}
			desc = lepsius.1501_taxonomy_cromagnon
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_neanderthalensis_systemized
			}
			desc = lepsius.1501_taxonomy_neanderthalensis
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_erectus_systemized
			}
			desc = lepsius.1501_taxonomy_erectus
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_australopithecus_systemized
			}
			desc = lepsius.1501_taxonomy_australopithecus
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = lepsius_paranthropus_systemized
			}
			desc = lepsius.1501_taxonomy_paranthropus
		}
		desc = lepsius.1501_miscellaneous
		desc = lepsius.1501_anthropological_prestige
		desc = lepsius.1501_global_total_human_fossils
	}

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_fossil_java.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_anthropology.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_cromagnon_systemizer
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_cromagnon_systemizer_country
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_neanderthalensis_systemizer
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_neanderthalensis_systemizer_country
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_erectus_systemizer
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_erectus_systemizer_country
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_australopithecus_systemizer
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_australopithecus_systemizer_country
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_paranthropus_systemizer
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_paranthropus_systemizer_country
		}
	}

	option = {	#Visit special Fossils
		name = lepsius.1501.g
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = dubois_fossil_java
					has_variable = dubois_fossil_neanderthaler
					has_variable = dubois_fossil_taung
					has_variable = dubois_fossil_peking
					has_variable = dubois_fossil_cromagnon
					has_variable = dubois_fossil_piltdown
				}
			}
		}

		trigger_event = {
			id = lepsius.1502
			popup = yes
		}
	}
	option = {	#Leave the Fossil Collection
		name = lepsius.1501.h
		remove_variable =  lepsius_visiting_human_evolution_var

		custom_tooltip = lepsius_leave_human_evolution_tt
	}

	after = {
		remove_variable = lepsius_total_unknown_human_fossils_var
	}
}
