#Lepsius 1601: A Donation (Intelligentsia, Egyptian Artifacts)

lepsius.1601 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1601.t
	desc = lepsius.1601.d
	flavor = lepsius.1601.f

	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:lepsius_donator_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	cooldown = {
		years = 35
	}

	trigger = {
		lepsius_has_archaeological_museum = yes
		ig:ig_intelligentsia = {
			is_marginal = no
		}
		has_global_variable = lepsius_archaeology_possible_global_var
	}

	immediate = {
		ig:ig_intelligentsia = {
			save_scope_as = intelligentsia_ig
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = lepsius_donator_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1601.g #A wonderful donation for our museum!
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_add_x_egyptian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 5 }
		scope:intelligentsia_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_benefactor_of_archaeology_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1601.h #This sycophant is just trying to take advantage.
		scope:intelligentsia_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_ignored_archaeological_donation_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
		every_interest_group = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					this = scope:intelligentsia_ig
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_incorruptible_realist_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		lepsius_update_exhibition_effect = yes
	}
}

lepsius.1604 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1601.t
	desc = lepsius.1604.d
	flavor = lepsius.1601.f

	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:lepsius_donator_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	cooldown = {
		years = 35
	}

	trigger = {
		lepsius_has_archaeological_museum = yes
		ig:ig_petty_bourgeoisie = {
			is_marginal = no
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		ig:ig_petty_bourgeoisie = {
			save_scope_as = petty_bourgeoisie_ig
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = lepsius_donator_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1601.g #A wonderful donation for our museum!
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_add_x_precolumbian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 5 }
		scope:petty_bourgeoisie_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_benefactor_of_archaeology_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1601.h #This sycophant is just trying to take advantage.
		scope:petty_bourgeoisie_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_ignored_archaeological_donation_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
		every_interest_group = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					this = scope:petty_bourgeoisie_ig
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_incorruptible_realist_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		lepsius_update_exhibition_effect = yes
	}
}

#Lepsius 1605: A Donation (Industrialists, Aegean Artifacts)

lepsius.1605 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1601.t
	desc = lepsius.1605.d
	flavor = lepsius.1601.f

	duration = 3

	}

			is_marginal = no
		}

	}

	immediate = {
		ig:ig_industrialists = {
			save_scope_as = industrialists_ig
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = lepsius_donator_scope
			}
		}
	}

		name = lepsius.1601.g #A wonderful donation for our museum!

		scope:industrialists_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_benefactor_of_archaeology_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1601.h #This sycophant is just trying to take advantage.
		scope:industrialists_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_ignored_archaeological_donation_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
		every_interest_group = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					this = scope:industrialists_ig
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_incorruptible_realist_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		lepsius_update_exhibition_effect = yes
	}
}

#Lepsius 1606: Egyptomania

lepsius.1606 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1606.t
	desc = lepsius.1606.d
	flavor = lepsius.1606.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/egypt/lepsius_egypt_cat.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	cooldown = {
		years = 25
	}

	trigger = {
		lepsius_has_archaeological_museum = yes
		var:lepsius_egyptian_artifact_minor >= 30
		any_interest_group = {
			is_in_government = no
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_interest_group = {
			limit = {
    			is_in_government = no
	        }
			save_scope_as = lepsius_esoteric_ig
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = lepsius_esoteric_leader
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1606.g #Let them indulge in their little cult.
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_egyptomania_modifier
			years = 5
		}
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = {
			AMOUNT = "12"
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				is_capital = yes
			}
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				pop_type = academics
				value = 0.1
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1606.h #Ban this humbug
		scope:lepsius_esoteric_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_intolerant_of_the_occlut_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 1607: Mayanism

lepsius.1607 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1607.t
	desc = lepsius.1607.d
	flavor = lepsius.1606.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/yucatan/lepsius_yucatan_plate5_copan.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	cooldown = {
		years = 25
	}

	trigger = {
		lepsius_has_archaeological_museum = yes
		var:lepsius_precolumbian_artifact_minor >= 30
		any_interest_group = {
			is_in_government = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_interest_group = {
			limit = {
    			is_in_government = no
	        }
			save_scope_as = lepsius_esoteric_ig
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = lepsius_esoteric_leader
			}
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_university
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_mayanism_state
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1606.g #Let them indulge in their little cult.
		default_option = yes
		scope:lepsius_esoteric_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_tolerant_of_the_occlut_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
		scope:lepsius_mayanism_state = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_mayanism_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1606.h #Ban this humbug
		scope:lepsius_mayanism_state = {
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				pop_type = academics
				value = 0.15
			}
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 1608: Panbabylonism

	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1608.t
	desc = lepsius.1608.d
	flavor = lepsius.1606.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/mesopotamia/lepsius_mesopotamia_gilgamesh.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	cooldown = {
		years = 25
	}

	trigger = {
		lepsius_has_archaeological_museum = yes
		var:lepsius_mesopotamian_artifact_minor >= 30
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1608.g #This is pseudo science!
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = lepsius_panbabylonism_modifier
			}
		}
		default_option = yes
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = {
			AMOUNT = "-12"
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1608.h #Great!
		trigger = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_panbabylonism_modifier
		}
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = {
			AMOUNT = "36"
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 1609: Atlantism

lepsius.1609 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1609.t
	desc = lepsius.1609.d
	flavor = lepsius.1606.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/greece/lepsius_greece_minoan_bull.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	cooldown = {
		years = 25
	}

	trigger = {
		lepsius_has_archaeological_museum = yes
		var:lepsius_aegean_artifact_minor >= 30
	}

	immediate = {
		random_interest_group = {
			limit = {
    			is_in_government = yes
	        }
			save_scope_as = lepsius_esoteric_ig
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = lepsius_esoteric_leader
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1608.g #This is pseudo science!
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = lepsius_atlantis_clue
			}
		}
		lepsius_small_add_technology = yes
		scope:lepsius_esoteric_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_intolerant_of_the_occlut_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1609.h #Who can say whether it's true or just a legend?
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = lepsius_atlantis_clue
			}
		}
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = {
			AMOUNT = "12"
		}
		scope:lepsius_esoteric_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_tolerant_of_the_occlut_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_government_belongs_to_cult_modifier
			years = 5
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1609.i #There is solid evidence of Atlantis
		trigger = {
			var:lepsius_atlantis_clue >= 1
		}
		lepsius_small_add_technology = yes
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = {
			AMOUNT = "12"
		}
		lepsius_add_x_aegean_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 3 }
		scope:lepsius_esoteric_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_tolerant_of_the_occlut_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		lepsius_update_exhibition_effect = yes
	}
}

	}

	}

		name = lepsius.1610.g #We'll invest
		default_option = yes

		add_treasury = -50000
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1610.h #It's not worth it.
	}
}

#Lepsius 1611: Ticket prices

lepsius.1611 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1611.t
	desc = lepsius.1611.d
	flavor = lepsius.1611.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/museum/lepsius_museum_interior.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	cooldown = {
		years = 25
	}

	trigger = {
		lepsius_has_archaeological_museum = yes
		OR = {
			var:lepsius_egyptian_artifact_minor >= 25
			var:lepsius_mesopotamian_artifact_minor >= 25
			var:lepsius_aegean_artifact_minor >= 25
			var:lepsius_precolumbian_artifact_minor >= 25
		}
		NOR = {
			has_modifier = lepsius_museum_high_prices_modifier
			has_modifier = lepsius_museum_no_prices_modifier
		}
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1611.g #Higher Ticket Prices
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_museum_high_prices_modifier
			years = 10
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1611.h #Lower the prices just a bit
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_museum_lower_prices_modifier
			years = 10
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1611.i #In fact, the entrance should be free.
		add_modifier = {
			name = lepsius_museum_no_prices_modifier
			years = 10
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_lepsius_archaeological_museum
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_open_museum_modifier
				years = 10
			}
		}
	}
}

#Lepsius 1612: Legacy of $Director$

lepsius.1612 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.1612.t
	desc = lepsius.1612.d
	flavor = lepsius.1612.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/museum/lepsius_museum_interior.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	cooldown = {
		years = 25
	}

	trigger = {
		lepsius_has_archaeological_museum = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		create_character = {
			interest_group = ig_intelligentsia
			save_scope_as = lepsius_director_scope
		}
		scope:lepsius_director_scope = {
			place_character_in_void = 120
			add_trait = lepsius_archaeologist
			add_trait = charismatic
			add_trait = bandit
		}
		random_list = {
			1 = { set_variable = lepsius_director_egyptian_var }
			1 = { set_variable = lepsius_director_mesopotamian_var }
			1 = { set_variable = lepsius_director_aegean_var }
			1 = { set_variable = lepsius_director_precolumbian_var }
			1 = { set_variable = lepsius_director_local_var }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1612.g #The truth must come out!
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_director_egyptian_var
			}
			lepsius_add_x_egyptian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 3 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_director_mesopotamian_var
			}
			lepsius_add_x_mesopotamian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 3 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_director_aegean_var
			}
			lepsius_add_x_aegean_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 3 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_director_precolumbian_var
			}
			lepsius_add_x_precolumbian_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 3 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_director_local_var
			}
			lepsius_add_x_local_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 3 }
		}
		ig:ig_intelligentsia = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_ruined_legacy_of_director_modifier
				years = 10
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.1612.h #$Director$ was a honorable man.
		ig:ig_intelligentsia = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_preserved_legacy_of_director_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		scope:lepsius_director_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = no
		}
		lepsius_update_exhibition_effect = yes
	}
}

#################################################################################

######Historical Archaeologists######
#Lepsius 2000: Thomsen invents the Three-Age System
lepsius.2000 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.2000.t
	desc = lepsius.2000.d
	flavor = lepsius.2000.f

	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:lepsius_new_archaeologist_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_variable = lepsius_three_age_system_invented_global_var }
		year > 1835
		c:DEN ?= this
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = lepsius_three_age_system_invented_global_var
		create_thomsen_cristian_jurgensen_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.2000.g #Such a great mind needs to work for us!
		default_option = yes

		lepsius_set_new_archaeologist_as_archaeologist_effect = yes

		scope:lepsius_new_archaeologist_scope = {
			set_variable = lepsius_archaeologist_invented_three_age_system_var
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_technology_researched = lepsius_antiquarianism_tech
				}
			}
			add_technology_researched = lepsius_antiquarianism_tech
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.2000.h #He can stay in his museum...
		default_option = yes

		lepsius_remove_new_archaeologist_effect = yes

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_technology_researched = lepsius_antiquarianism_tech
				}
			}
			add_technology_researched = lepsius_antiquarianism_tech
		}

		lepsius_large_add_technology = yes
	}
}

######Local Archaeological Events######

### Roman Empire ###
#Lepsius 2101: Remains of a Roman Battle
lepsius.2101 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:lepsius_local_archaeological_state_scope

	title = lepsius.2101.t
	desc = lepsius.2101.d
	flavor = lepsius.2101.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/lepsius_pictures/lepsius_local_roman/lepsius_roman_battle.dds"
	}
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
		lepsius_has_active_archaeologist = yes
		any_scope_state = {
			lepsius_imperium_romanum_archaeology_region = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_imperium_romanum_archaeology_region = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_local_archaeological_state_scope
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.2101.g #Not a prestigeous, but an important discovery!
		default_option = yes

		lepsius_add_x_local_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 5 }
	}

	after = {
		lepsius_update_exhibition_effect = yes
	}
}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
		has_technology_researched = lepsius_modern_archaeology_tech
		lepsius_has_active_archaeologist = yes
		any_scope_state = {
			lepsius_imperium_romanum_archaeology_region = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				lepsius_imperium_romanum_archaeology_region = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = lepsius_local_archaeological_state_scope
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.2103.g #Not all treasure is made of silver and gold!
		default_option = yes

		lepsius_add_x_local_artifacts_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 20 }
	}

	after = {
		lepsius_update_exhibition_effect = yes
	}
}

######Archaeologist Events (without interactions)######

#Lepsius 2500: New Archaeological Map of [State]
lepsius.2500 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:lepsius_local_archaeological_state_scope

	title = lepsius.2500.t
	desc = lepsius.2500.d
	flavor = lepsius.2500.f

	duration = 3

	cooldown = {
		years = { 15 25 }
	}

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:lepsius_archaeologist_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
		lepsius_has_active_archaeologist = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_local_archaeological_state_scope
		}
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = { #This will open doors to new finds!
		name = lepsius.2500.g
		default_option = yes

		lepsius_small_add_technology = yes
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 15 }
	}

	after = {
		lepsius_update_exhibition_effect = yes
	}
}

######Archaeologist Events with interactions to other Scientists######

#Lepsius 2600: The lost Star
lepsius.2600 = {
	type = country_event

	title = lepsius.2600.t
	desc = lepsius.2600.d
	flavor = lepsius.2600.f

	duration = 3

	cooldown = {
		years = { 15 25 }
	}

	gui_window = event_window_2char

	left_icon = scope:lepsius_archaeologist_scope
	right_icon = scope:verrier_astronomer_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_archaeology.dds"

	trigger = {
		lepsius_has_active_archaeologist = yes
		verrier_has_astronomer = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_archaeologist_scope
		}
		var:verrier_astronomer_var = {
			save_scope_as = verrier_astronomer_scope
		}
	}

	option = { #A tremendous scientific discovery!
		name = lepsius.2600.g
		default_option = yes

		verrier_add_x_astronomical_objects_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		archaeologist_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 10 }
		astronomer_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 10 }
	}

	after = {
		lepsius_update_exhibition_effect = yes
	}
}
